Page 5

Current Commentary

Future Sino-Japanese Negotiations

— Should

Kuwashima, the director of the East Asia Bureau of the Japanese Foreign Ministry, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. He is to convey the new instructions recently decided upon by Prime Minister Hirota and the three ministers of the Army, Navy, and Foreign Affairs to Ambassador Kawagoe. There is renewed hope for the continuation of the interrupted Sino-Japanese negotiations to adjust diplomatic relations. What is the content of the new instructions brought by Kuwashima? Because both parties are maintaining strict secrecy, we have no way of knowing. However, judging from the current situation, we can also speculate that the negotiating policy indicated by the new instructions may be more moderate in nature and smaller in scope than all the demands already made by Kawagoe. But at its core, it must still contain a full spirit of aggression. In the Sino-Japanese negotiations on the 23rd of last month, our government clearly rejected Ambassador Kawagoe's demands. Since then, the Japanese army in North China has been preparing for large-scale exercises of a demonstrative nature. The Japanese Marines in Shanghai even extended their security lines to the banks of the Suzhou Creek. And the Japanese authorities have repeatedly claimed that they are prepared to take effective measures when necessary. A dangerous haze is indeed gathering in the skies of the Far East, endangering peace. However, discerning people can easily determine that using force at this juncture is extremely unfavorable to Japan. Now China has completed a unified situation politically, economically, and militarily. In terms of the public, patriotic sentiment has also risen to an extreme. As for Japan, not only is its finances without a way out, but also its international relations with other powers in the Far East have not improved. As everyone knows, Japan is accustomed to taking shortcuts. Unless it seizes an opportunity like the one in the September 18th Incident, it will not easily use force. It certainly does not want to go to war with China at this time. The Japanese authorities' spreading of war atmosphere, as the foreign press in Tokyo reported, is merely a threatening tactic to instigate the independence of North China. This time Kuwashima's arrival in China indicates that Japan intends to change its approach. Japan should modify its negotiating policy to be more 'reasonable.'

However, Japan's fundamental national policy is to expand its influence in China. No matter how 'reasonable' it modifies its negotiating policy, it cannot but infringe upon China's independent sovereignty. Moreover, now it is Kuwashima, the drafter of the Hirota Three Principles, who has brought the new instructions, and the threatening situation has not diminished. How can we expect Japan to have any fundamental modification of its policy toward China? However, in the current situation, if Japan wants to break the diplomatic deadlock, it cannot but consider the factor that has always played a significant role in Sino-Japanese issues, namely Britain. Therefore, it is very possible that it will modify its negotiating policy to a 'reasonable' degree that can gain British understanding. We remember Sir Otto Niemeyer's farewell advice to China to revise its tariffs. We know that the conservative elements in Britain have always regarded the emerging Japan as an important force to check the United States and Russia and may tacitly approve of Japan's free actions in North China. We also know that Britain is determined not to let war break out between China and Japan. So, can Japan's current negotiating policy seek a compromise with Britain? This is indeed a question that deserves our attention.

Based on the above, we cannot be too optimistic about future Sino-Japanese negotiations. Nor can we be too optimistic about the British authorities' close concern for the current situation in China.

French Communist Party Congress, Anti-Fascist Demonstrations, Unite to Uphold Democracy, Right-Wing Crowds Resist Demonstrations, 1,000 Arrested and Immediately Released

(Paris) The Communist Party's demonstration congress was originally scheduled to begin at 3:00 PM, but by 2:30 PM, all the podiums and seats in the Prince's Park stadium were already full, with an audience of 40,000 people, leaving almost no space. First, Communist Party leader Senator Cachin delivered a speech, saying, "The world is in turmoil, and the tide of Fascism is sweeping through various countries. Only France is still the only country with democratic politics. This is thanks to the strength of the Popular Front. The French Popular Front is based on 7 million workers, with 5 million already joining the General Confederation of Labor. This is why the Popular Front is so powerful." Then, Deputy Speaker of the Chamber of Deputies, Duclos, delivered a speech, saying that any attempt to divide the Popular Front was a "destructive policy." Regarding the devaluation of the franc, he said, "Our party, in order to alleviate the poverty of the people, has already stipulated in the Popular Front's program a method to reform the tax system based on democratic principles. This method was not adopted, and instead, it was replaced by currency devaluation, which our party did not approve of. The reason why our party voted in favor of the currency bill in the parliament was to maintain the Popular Front." Then, Communist Party Deputy Malter delivered a speech. Having recently returned from an investigation in Spain, Malter specifically defended against various slanders by foreign countries against the Spanish Republican government, and said that the Spanish rebels were receiving large amounts of military supplies from Italy and Germany, and that effective action should be taken immediately to lift the blockade against the Spanish government. He also said, "The French Fascist Party, after being completely defeated in the elections on May 3rd of this year, has been attacking the republican system and the French people with all its might. Therefore, we must unite our forces to complete the program of the Popular Front." Finally, Communist Party Secretary General Dorais delivered a speech, praising the various actions of the Chamber of Deputies and the government that benefited the working class, but said, "We must now pay attention to ensuring that these measures are strictly implemented. Workers' wages must be guaranteed, and unjustified price increases must be prohibited. The connection between the middle class and the general public is the most beneficial guarantee for both parties. Any concession to the reactionaries will inevitably lead to further encroachments. Taking the devaluation of the franc as an example, the only ones who will suffer losses will be the poor families. Therefore, I sincerely advise my comrades in the Socialist Party that if we make many promises beforehand but do not deliver on them afterward, causing most people to be disappointed, the result will inevitably allow those who specialize in empty rhetoric and intend to destroy to take advantage of the situation. This is why democratic politics in Germany and Austria failed. The lessons of the past are a warning. The Popular Front must not repeat the same mistakes." Regarding the Spanish issue, Dorais also said, "The government's neutral attitude toward the Spanish events is a disgrace. Surrendering to Fascism will not only fail to save peace, but will also harm it." (4th, Havas News Agency)

(Paris) The western district of Paris is a residential area for wealthy households. West of the Porte d'Auteuil is the famous Bois de Boulogne, with its dense forests and beautiful scenery, a place where Parisians usually relax and enjoy holidays. It is usually quiet and secluded, without the bustling atmosphere of the city. However, it has recently been transformed into a center of political demonstrations, with crowds of people moving about and shouting constantly, a truly rare phenomenon. The Communist Party held a demonstration congress in Prince's Park outside the Porte d'Auteuil this afternoon. Arrangements had been made in advance, and the Social Problems Research Association organized by Fascist leader Colonel de la Rocque also held a counter-demonstration at the same time. Although the government had issued a ban beforehand, it was not canceled. It is estimated that 40,000 people participated in the Communist Party's demonstration congress this afternoon, while 15,000 people participated in the Fascist counter-demonstration. Fortunately, the police maintained order, so the two sides did not engage in direct conflict, nor did any serious incidents occur, which was also fortunate. At noon today, the quiet area of western Paris was already crowded with people. Public and private cars, as well as underground trains, brought in passengers, thousands upon thousands, in an endless stream. At 1:00 PM, 2,000 demonstrators from the Social Problems Research Association arrived in formation, led by right-wing Deputy Grilys, and were dispersed by the police. At 4:00 PM, the Porte d'Auteuil square was extremely crowded, but no incidents occurred. Fascist Party demonstrators tried to break into the venue of the Communist Party's demonstration congress in Prince's Park, but were stopped by the police. A large number of people were arrested and temporarily detained in various police stations in the 14th arrondissement. At 5:45 PM, someone threw a flower vase at the police on the street from a cafe on Auteuil Street, and then used water bottles as weapons, throwing them into the center of the street. The police immediately drove the crowd out of the cafe and arrested many people. At around 6:00 PM, the crowd participating in the congress in Prince's Park began to exit. Thanks to the effective protection of the police, no conflict occurred with the Fascist crowd. By 7:00 PM in the evening, the crowd gradually dispersed, and the Auteuil area returned to calm. After the incident, a total of 1,300 people were arrested. Except for ten of them who were temporarily detained for illegally carrying weapons, the rest were released. Most of those arrested were members of the Social Problems Research Association, many of whom came from other provinces. The police authorities did not find out that a large number of people had come to Paris from various provinces this morning to participate in the Fascist counter-demonstration, because the Fascist Party felt that there were not enough people in Paris, so it temporarily mobilized people from various provinces. During today's demonstration, two members of the crowd and two police officers were injured and sent to the hospital. In addition, several police officers and members of the crowd suffered minor injuries and left after being bandaged at the pharmacy. There were no other major incidents. In addition, taxi drivers complained to the police that their cars were pelted with stones while carrying Communist Party members to Prince's Park for the meeting. There were a total of thirty such incidents. (4th, Havas News Agency)

Conflicts Between Left and Right Wings in London, Stones and Glass Bottles Used as Weapons, Police Suppression, Many Arrested

(London) British Fascist Party members marched in formation in the East End of London yesterday, injuring several people and arresting 84. When the incident first occurred on Royal Mint Street, the authorities, fearing that the demonstration would cause riots, immediately dispatched 5,000 special police officers to the area to suppress the unrest. The police had no choice but to use batons to disperse the crowd, resulting in injuries to several people, nine of whom were seriously injured and sent to the hospital for treatment. Soon after, Sir Oswald Mosley, the leader of the British Fascist Party, arrived and met with Police Commissioner Sir Game, who informed him that Fascist Party members were not allowed to march in the East End and were only allowed to pass through Blackfriars and disperse at Embankment. Subsequently, a large crowd attempted to rescue someone who had been arrested on Leman Street, and the police again used batons to suppress the unrest. The rioters were extremely violent, throwing stones and sharp objects at the police. Yesterday, many Fascist Party members drove cars through the streets, with iron mesh on the windows of the cars. Afterwards, Jewish and labor groups filed serious protests with the authorities, opposing the Fascist Party's demonstrations. The Jewish National Council submitted a document to the Home Office petitioning to ban Fascist Party members from demonstrating, with a total of 100,000 signatures. This morning, all newspapers detailed the riots that occurred during the Fascist Party members' demonstration in the East End yesterday. Newspapers estimated that 2,500 Fascist Party members participated, and 6,000 police officers suppressed the unrest. There were also 100,000 anti-Fascist Party members who joined in the protests. The worst riots occurred in the Stepney area. Fascist Party members robbed the lumberyard of a contractor on a street in the area and blocked the street with a loaded truck and paving stones. When the police arrived, the Party members threw stones and broken bottles at them, and threw garbage and wooden chairs out of the windows, and set off blank cartridges and firecrackers to scare the horses of the mounted police. The ground was littered with broken glass and stones to hinder the police's actions. The police repeatedly swung their batons to disperse the crowd, injuring several people. The street was eventually cleared. After the incident, various weapons were found, including iron bars, chair legs wrapped in barbed wire, and broken glass bottles. Fascist Party members now claim that the authorities' decision to ban the Party's march is a surrender to "Red terror." The Communist Party said that Fascist Party leader Sir Oswald Mosley has suffered the most shameful defeat. (5th, Reuters)

Mussolini Announces 40% Devaluation of Italian Currency, Strict Measures to Prevent Price Hikes, Tax Reductions on Imports of Food and Fuel

(Rome) The Italian Cabinet decided today to devalue the Italian lira by about 40%, with the exchange rate set at 90 lire to one pound sterling and 19 lire to one US dollar. The Cabinet also decided to reduce import duties to prevent price spikes. The import duty reduction for wheat is from 75 lire to 45 lire per 100 pounds, for fresh meat from livestock is reduced by 60%, for livestock it is reduced by 65%, for coal it is reduced from 10 lire to 5 lire per ton, for charcoal it is reduced from 42.5 lire to 30 lire per ton, and import duties on other food and raw materials are also reduced or even eliminated. (5th, National Telegram)

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini announced the devaluation of the Italian lira after this morning's cabinet meeting, with its new value set at 92 lire to one pound sterling and 19 lire to one US dollar. As for the amount of pure gold contained in the lira, it has also been stipulated that each 100 lire contains 4.677 grams of pure gold, whereas previously the amount of pure gold in each 100 lire was 7.9191 grams. Mussolini also announced that the tariffs on various essential necessities, including food and coal, will be reduced. The gold reserves of the Bank of Italy have been revalued according to the new parity and the difference paid by the Treasury. Landowners will be notified to purchase new 5% government bonds worth 5% of the net value of their property to offset the currency devaluation. Rents, gas, electricity, and public and private transportation services will not be increased for two years. Hotel or apartment owners who charge excessive prices will be severely punished. In addition, strict measures have been taken to manage the cost of food and other necessities of life. (5th, Reuters)

Italian Economic Policy Leans Toward Liberalism

(Rome) Although Italy's economic policy will continue to aim at self-sufficiency, as it did when the Italian-Abyssinian war began last October, in other words, the foreign trade policy will still be determined with reference to national defense needs, it is already more inclined towards liberalism. This can be seen from the Prime Minister's approval of the temporary suspension of the current restrictions on capital flows and foreign exchange. In short, although the date of full restoration of economic liberalism cannot be determined, it is clear that the new monetary policy has liberalism as its ultimate goal. (5th, Havas News Agency)

Running Counter to Germany

From an economic point of view, England and Italy are currently negotiating a trade treaty, and the negotiations will naturally be affected. British importers expect the prices of Italian agricultural products, wines, and rayon fabrics to decrease soon. However, British farmers, in order to protect their agricultural products, may demand that the government increase import taxes to counteract this. However, if Italy can follow France and reduce import tax rates, then it will be a different matter. (Havas, 5th)

London Not Surprised

(London) Foreign exchange traders here did not express much surprise at Italy's decision to devalue its currency. Although some hinted that the extent of Italy's devaluation seemed greater than they had anticipated, the general opinion is that from a technical point of view, the lira market will not be materially affected because transactions involving the lira are strictly controlled. British merchants generally welcome Italy's reduction of import taxes on raw materials, but believe that the immediate benefits of the tax reduction are limited because merchants are unwilling to continue selling on credit to Italy before the previous debts are cleared. Currently, negotiations on clearing old debts are underway in Rome. (Reuters, 5th)

France Appeals to the World: Reduce Tariff Barriers, Economic Prosperity May Be Expected; Establish a Committee to Control Domestic Prices

(Paris) French Minister of Economy, Mr. Spinasse, appealed to all countries in the world via radio broadcast today to emulate France's example in reducing tariff barriers. It is said that international commercial meetings have begun and will be completed within a few weeks. At that time, the world's prosperity will surely become a reality. Before Mr. Spinasse gave this radio address, the French government ordered the establishment of a tariff commission to handle matters such as controlling prices, reducing import tariffs, various taxes and license fees, and relaxing quotas. (Reuters, 5th)

(Paris) Minister of Economy Spinasse recently delivered a radio broadcast speech, strongly arguing that currency devaluation will not cause prices to rise. The past examples of England, the United States, and Belgium can be used as evidence. In terms of bread, milk, and wine, which are daily necessities for the people, their national distribution will not be affected by currency devaluation. However, the prices of some foreign goods may increase slightly, but goods imported from Switzerland and Belgium are an exception, because the currencies of Switzerland and Belgium have devalued along with the French currency. Spinasse went on to explain that the government has established price monitoring committees in various provinces to monitor price fluctuations in various places and take effective measures at any time to prevent price increases. (Havas, 4th)

The British government is currently taking two measures to promote the world's economic recovery. First, although the currencies of other countries have depreciated, the British import tax will not be increased as a result. Opening of the International Labor Organization Maritime Conference; Speech and Proposals of Our Country's Representative, Zhao Banfu

Berlin Correspondence: The 21st International Labor Conference Maritime Session is scheduled to open on October 6th. The Chinese labor representative designated by the government is Zhao Banfu. The speech given by Mr. Zhao at the conference, as well as our country's proposals, are recorded separately below.

Speech at the Conference: Gentlemen, I am honored and delighted to participate in this International Labor Conference Maritime Session. Under the ardent hope of hardworking seafarers around the world, this conference brings together representatives of governments, employers, and labor from various countries to uphold justice and humanity. I respectfully represent all Chinese seafarers in celebrating the success of the conference and hope that the conference's work will not only satisfy seafarers in China and around the world but also eliminate the detrimental effects of international economic competition on seafarers. The director's report has clearly analyzed the situation of seafarers around the world. Regarding the situation of Chinese seafarers, I would like to take this opportunity to add a few words. Since various imperialists successively obtained navigation rights on Chinese inland waterways, Chinese seafarers have been employed by foreign shipping companies. Because their labor is cheap, and it is convenient for trade and transportation to and from China, their numbers have increased daily for over a century. Almost the entire world bears the footprints of Chinese seafarers. In 1922 (i.e., the 11th year of the Republic of China), Chinese seafarers, seeking to improve inequality in treatment and eliminate the contractor system, launched a large-scale strike on January 13th. I believe that those of you dedicated to social peace still remember this unprecedented chapter in the history of the struggle for a livelihood. After the Paris Peace Conference, Chinese seafarers hoped for international regulations on equal treatment and have been eagerly anticipating this day. However, for more than a decade, the hopes of Chinese seafarers have not made the slightest progress, and some foreign shipping companies, especially foreign shipping companies based in China, have become increasingly harsh in their treatment of Chinese seafarers. Now, I would like to mention some of the most prominent examples for your consideration. As mentioned above, the great strike of Chinese seafarers on January 13, 1922, aimed to improve unequal treatment and eliminate the contractor system. Chinese seafarers hate unequal treatment for the same work and the exploitation of the contractor system more than poisonous snakes and fierce beasts. Although the strike resulted in a victory for the seafarers, the shipping companies not only failed to fulfill their promises afterward but also gradually intensified their practices as time passed. Until now, their procedures for employing Chinese seafarers do not seek healthy and legitimate Chinese seafarer unions but directly negotiate extremely harsh employment terms with contractor bosses who aim to profit and exploit. The seafarers themselves have no freedom to choose ships, and they have absolutely no opportunity to participate in the content of the employment terms. Thus, the contractor bosses, on the one hand, obtain the most arduous labor for the shipping companies at the lowest wages and, on the other hand, routinely demand various introduction fees from the seafarers. Under this double exploitation, it is impossible for seafarers to secure a basic livelihood, leading to frequent suicides. In addition to using contractor bosses to squeeze cheap labor from seafarers, shipping companies also force seafarers to pay a deposit ranging from 300 to 700 yuan per person. Faced with the fear of unemployment, seafarers have no choice but to borrow at the highest interest rates to pay the deposit. The wages of Chinese seafarers are low, with the highest being no more than 44 yuan per month and the lowest being only 8 yuan per month. It is impossible to maintain the livelihood of their families or themselves, let alone pay interest. Gentlemen, if this tragic situation is not immediately addressed, the consequences for Chinese seafarers, driven by the demands of survival, are unimaginable. From an economic perspective and from the perspective of human peace, if the issue of equal treatment is not regulated and inhumane and illegal systems are not eliminated, capitalists, having so many advantages to exploit, will inevitably employ low-cost seafarers as much as possible to engage in international or private enterprise competition. As a result, not only will Chinese seafarers be forever reduced to a life of servitude, but seafarers from all countries will also suffer greatly. Because capitalists, on the one hand, obtain the most arduous labor of Chinese seafarers at the lowest cost and, on the other hand, will inevitably deceive or reduce the employment of their own high-cost seafarers as much as possible. In recent years, the world's economic and unemployment crises have become increasingly severe. Chinese seafarers residing abroad are subject to discrimination by local governments and exclusion by local seafarers of the same class. Although there are many reasons for this, the common sentiment is that Chinese seafarers have taken away their livelihoods. As such, racial discrimination and animosity arise among seafarers. How can one hope for human peace? Gentlemen, we are all here to seek human peace. We cannot sit idly by and ignore the increasingly severe trend of human conflict. We must recognize that the path to human peace cannot be built by labor, capital, or government alone. It requires the enlightened and unified efforts of everyone. To break this crisis, I believe that the only way is to immediately ensure equal treatment for Chinese seafarers. In addition, I have one more matter to report to you. In June 1927 (i.e., the 16th year of the Republic of China), the Hong Kong government, citing the pretext of Communist Party disturbances, closed the Hong Kong branch of the Chinese Seafarers' Union. In recent years, despite repeated negotiations with the Hong Kong government, the results have been zero. Freedom of association for workers is permitted by the laws of civilized countries around the world. The Chinese Seafarers' Union, under the supervision of Chinese government laws, is an organization that protects the economic interests of seafarers. Whether the Hong Kong government's refusal to allow the restoration of the Hong Kong branch is due to a misunderstanding that the Chinese Seafarers' Union is an organization with political functions or whether the policy of the Hong Kong government, which claims to be governed by law and civilization, does not allow for a legitimate seafarers' organization, is a mystery that I cannot understand. Chinese seafarers cherish peace and, unless absolutely necessary, do not wish to have a second "1922" great strike. Therefore, they have endured and tolerated for ten years. Today, I represent the Chinese seafarers of my country in requesting the assistance of international justice. I hope that the International Labor Office will also provide strong assistance to Chinese seafarers on this issue. Finally, I solemnly declare that Chinese seafarers fully support the work and policies of the International Labor Organization and believe that the International Labor Conference is the gateway to human peace and all justice, and will give a satisfactory answer to seafarers in China and around the world.

Proposals by the Chinese Representative: 1. Regarding the issue of equal treatment for domestic and foreign seafarers, please decide to include it in the agenda of the next session and promptly draft a convention. (Explanation) In 1936, the 20th International Labor Conference discussed "The Recruitment and Placement of Migrant Workers" submitted by the Labor Office, and the conference decided to include it in the agenda of the 1938 conference. In particular, regarding the issue of equal treatment for migrant workers, the conference made great efforts to promote the principles of human peace, equality, and justice. The work of seafarers is related to life safety and public interest, and its difficulty and burden are no less than that of ordinary workers, and it does not differ due to racial differences. Seafarers have been awaiting international regulations on fair treatment for sixteen years. From an economic point of view, if the issue of equal treatment is not jointly negotiated internationally, shipowners of countries with higher wages will inevitably employ seafarers from countries with lower wages as much as possible to engage in international or private enterprise competition. To avoid sacrificing seafarers to engage in such competition, this issue cannot be ignored any longer. Also, the 13th Maritime Conference in October 1929 passed the following resolution: "The issue of equal treatment for Asian seafarers should be placed on the agenda as soon as possible, and the Labor Office should pay attention to the investigation of this fact." Although the passage of this proposal only mentions Asian seafarers, its spirit and effect are to seek human peace and eliminate international or private competition. Its importance has already been recognized by the conference. Based on the above explanation, please decide to include this issue in the agenda of the next session and draft a convention. 2. Please suggest that relevant member states assist the Chinese government and the Chinese Seafarers' Union in effectively eliminating the contractor system. (Explanation) The contractor system is the most inhumane system for exploiting workers, which needs no explanation. The 2nd and 9th Maritime Conferences in 1920 and 1926 respectively formulated two draft conventions, "Facilitating the Employment of Seafarers" and "Conditions of Seafarer Employment Contracts". The spirit of these two draft conventions is to protect the interests of seafarers during employment so that they are not contracted by agencies or individuals for profit and exploitation. The meaning is very clear. Since the Chinese government established its capital in Nanjing, it has strictly prohibited the contractor system. But the most unfortunate thing at present is that some foreign shipping companies, especially foreign shipping companies based in China, negotiate all their procedures for employing Chinese seafarers with contractor bosses, with extremely harsh employment conditions. The seafarers themselves have no freedom to choose ships, and they have absolutely no opportunity to participate in the content of the employment terms. The contractor bosses, in addition to demanding various introduction fees from the seafarers, also demand them from the companies. On the company side, because they can obtain the most arduous labor at the lowest wages, they are happy to pay the introduction fees. Although they are taken directly from the company, they are still taken indirectly from the seafarers, and the company still has surplus profits to be made. Faced with the fear of unemployment, seafarers have no choice but to seek a basic livelihood through layers of exploitation, but as a result, their lives cannot be secured, leading to frequent suicides. The occurrence of such inhumane and illegal facts is a regret for social justice and the conference. It should be suggested that relevant member states assist the Chinese government and the Chinese Seafarers' Union and warn their foreign shipping companies based in China to effectively eliminate it. 3. Please suggest that relevant member states assist the Chinese Seafarers' Union in effectively eliminating the deposit system. (Explanation) Chinese seafarers who serve in various foreign shipping companies based in China, in addition to being contracted by illegal contractor systems, are also required by the companies to pay a deposit ranging from 300 to 700 yuan per person. Faced with the fear of unemployment, seafarers have no choice but to borrow at the highest interest rates to pay the deposit, resulting in their monthly salary income being insufficient to maintain their livelihood after paying interest. The salaries of Chinese seafarers are low, with the highest being no more than 44 yuan per month and the lowest being only 8 yuan per month, and they must provide their own meals. With such meager treatment, it is already impossible to maintain the minimum livelihood of their families or themselves, let alone the exploitation of the contractor system and the deposit system. We urge all of you at the conference to pay close attention to the cruelty of this issue, suggest that relevant member states earnestly warn their foreign shipping companies based in China, and assist the Chinese Seafarers' Union in effectively eliminating it.

Zou Lu Returns to China and Arrives in Guangzhou; Fell Ill En Route and is Resting at Home for Several Days; Zou Advocates Transforming the Foundational Concepts of Education; Replacing Utilitarianism with the Teachings of Benevolence and Love

Guangzhou Correspondence: Zou Lu, a standing committee member of the Central Executive Committee and president of Sun Yat-sen University, has been abroad for four months. Recently, after attending the Third World Education Conference and participating in the 550th Anniversary Celebration of the University of Heidelberg in Germany, he began his return journey. He initially boarded the Italian ship "Conte Verde." However, when passing through Singapore, the ship's machinery was damaged, and he transferred to the British postal ship "Carthage" to sail eastward. On the 30th, he arrived in Hong Kong. Zou's staff and comrades had been waiting in Hong Kong to welcome him. Members of the Guangdong Party, military, political, and academic circles who went to Hong Kong to welcome him included Hu Wencan, Luo Yiqun, Wu Zhimei, Li Xiangen, Xiang Hanping, Xie Yibang, Li Xiaosheng, Chen Ce, Tan Huiquan, Zou Zhuoran, Zheng Yanfen, He Yanyan, Liu Jiwen, and others, numbering over a hundred. At approximately 1:00 PM that afternoon, the "Carthage" slowly docked at the Kowloon Wharf. Mr. Zou, ailing, emerged to greet those who had come to welcome him. Due to the arduous journey, he had fallen ill several days prior. However, he shook hands and exchanged greetings with those who welcomed him, speaking normally. Afterward, he went directly to the welcome reception hosted by seven Hong Kong organizations. Due to his discomfort, Mr. Zou did not give any interviews to reporters. He only handed over a written statement on educational philosophy, advocating for the reform of the foundational concepts of education, to the newspapers for publication. The statement's main points are: "The mission of education is not only to provide knowledge to the current society but also to create benefits for humanity. If it only provides knowledge to the current society, then in this world of the survival of the fittest, education at all levels and all sciences will only increase the ferocity of its sharp teeth and claws. In fact, all countries are currently preparing for war. Directly, this is through the increase and improvement of armaments. Indirectly, all food, transportation, industry, and other aspects are preparing for war. What promotes its authority for war is education. This is no different from politicians and militarists wanting to kill, and educators preparing excellent executioners and excellent killing knives for them. In this situation, if another major war occurs in the world, humanity will inevitably die at the hands of the executioners prepared by educators. The reason education has achieved this result is due to the erroneous foundational philosophy of education, driving humanity towards the path of war. If this foundational philosophical thought is not improved and created by education, then a world of humans devouring each other will inevitably be seen in the future. Therefore, the responsibility of educators at present must extend beyond the scope of current society and seek happiness for future humanity. The path to achieve this is to integrate the essential meanings of love for humanity from various religions and scholars in the past, and to integrate and organize them using scientific methods. With the ultimate goal of universal harmony, establish a philosophical foundation of extending oneself to others, benevolence to the people, and love for all things, to replace the current world's philosophy of competition and mutual struggle. In this way, the cruel devastation of war can be eliminated through educational philosophy, and humanity can obtain the most advanced science in this philosophical foundation of benevolence and love, for production, for distribution, for growth, for education, and for nourishment. Then education will truly bring benefits to humanity and will also have meaning. Whether education brings happiness or disaster to humanity depends entirely on the 'shift' in the purpose of education," etc. Due to his illness, Mr. Zou could not stay in Hong Kong for long. He boarded the "Tianyi" ship the next morning to return to Guangdong Province. Several hundred representatives from the Party, political, and academic circles in Guangdong Province were waiting at the pier to welcome him, carrying banners with slogans such as "Welcome Principal Zou back to the University" and "Welcome Committee Member Zou back to the Country," lined up on both sides of the road, creating a lively atmosphere. At 2:30 PM, the "Tianyi" ship docked, and Mr. Zou went ashore. He shook hands with each of the welcoming representatives. He then drove back to his private residence on Dongdi Road to rest. The welcoming party drove their cars, waving flags and setting off firecrackers, following behind to celebrate. After returning to his private residence, Zou first sent Xiao Guanying as his representative to Sun Yat-sen University in Shipai to meet with the deans of the various colleges and inquire about the recent situation of the university. It is reported that Zou, still recovering from his illness, has temporarily declined various social engagements and will return to the university to resume his duties after he recovers. (October 3rd)

Jiading

Widespread Malignant Malaria

Since January, malignant malaria has been prevalent in various villages, affecting two to three-tenths of the entire population. The symptoms are similar to those of a sudden illness, with no chills, and the fever does not decrease after sweating. It often takes more than ten days to recover, and many people have died. Doctors are making rounds day and night, unable to keep up. Poor patients cannot even afford to seek medical treatment. Pharmacies are also making double the profit.

Wuxi

Expanding Air Defense Propaganda

The Wuxi Air Defense Exhibition has been in preparation for many days. All kinds of equipment have been arranged in various exhibition rooms in the park for days. All the staff are extremely busy. Yesterday afternoon, the propaganda group of the exhibition held its first group meeting at the county education bureau. Those who attended were Zhang Manyu and Liang Zhiping, instructors of the air defense exhibition, Wang Zhaolong, director of the education bureau, Xu Chizi, head of the propaganda group of the air defense exhibition, and more than ten principals of primary and secondary schools. The meeting was chaired by Xu Chizi, and the following resolutions were made: (1) to formulate the number of propagandists assigned to each school and to determine the principles for selecting team leaders and members; (2) to have the propagandists from each school watch an air defense film at the Zhongnan Theater on October 7th from 8:00 AM to 9:30 AM. After 10:00 AM, the propagandists will receive instruction from the organizers of the air defense exhibition and then depart to give speeches; (3) to schedule the team members to gather at the park on October 9th at 3:30 PM to visit the air defense exhibition; and (4) to determine the locations for the speech teams from each school to give their speeches. The association also believes that the designated areas for each propaganda team are not yet comprehensive enough. In addition to carrying out practical propaganda in the tentatively designated locations, each school should further carry out propaganda in nearby other townships and towns to expand the propaganda force. From the 8th to the 14th of this month, 200 speech teams will be temporarily formed, organized by 1,000 team members. Each team will have one team leader and four team members. Each school will have one chief captain, who will be a faculty member. At 5:00 PM, the association also invited the deputy editors of various newspapers, including Jiang Dabai, Zhu Bingdie, Yu Shaozhou, Sun Boliang, and Zhang Rongliang. The association's instructor, Zhang Manyu, hosted them. Regarding the publication of special air defense supplements in various newspapers, it was decided that special air defense supplements would be published in the deputy sections of various newspapers starting on October 10th. The content will focus on air defense construction. Each newspaper will publish continuously for five days.

Changshu

Police Arrest Female Opium Trafficker at Station

The county government of this county suddenly received a phone call from Shanghai, stating that a female opium trafficker was carrying a large amount of smuggled opium and would be arriving in Changshu. After receiving the call, the county government immediately ordered officials from the anti-smoking section to accompany patrol captains from the Public Security Bureau to meet the train and conduct an inspection. Near Taicang Station, they found a carriage containing only a woman. She identified herself as Ma Wu. Two hemp bags were found on the roof of the carriage, filled with smuggled opium, estimated to be over two hundred taels. They were immediately taken to the county government. She confessed to the names of her accomplices, Zhang Maoli, the Zhang Maochun brothers, and Ma Changsheng. Unexpectedly, when they arrived at their destination, Zhang Maokui and Ma had already heard the news and fled. Only Zhang Maochun was still ill and was found in bed when the case was discovered. He could not escape and died of fright in bed. When the police went to arrest him, not only was there no one at home, but no one claimed the body. Currently, the county government plans to transfer the female opium trafficker Ma Wu to the Wuxi District Security Command for investigation.

Haizhou

Notorious Bandit Chen Bujin Arrested

Chen Bujin, also known as Xiao Yejiji, from Gaoyou, has been a bandit for many years. He was arrested in Shuyang County last month. The county government repeatedly interrogated him, and he confessed to robbery. Recently, the Gaoyou County government received a report and sent personnel to Shuyang to bring him back to Gaoyou for interrogation. According to reports, Chen led hundreds of bandits in the Gaoyou area, burning, killing, and looting, running rampant without restraint. He personally killed over a hundred people. There were numerous accusations against him, and the Gaoyou County government had offered a reward of 1,500 yuan for his arrest. He had been arrested several times, but he had either escaped en route or broken out of prison and fled. This time, he was arrested in Shuyang, and he will surely be publicly executed to eliminate this scourge.

Shen Yugong Discusses the World Games Basketball: Our Country's Failure, Still Don't Understand the Tournament Rules, Dong Shouyi Should Bear Considerable Responsibility

After the news of our country's basketball team's disastrous defeat in the World Games spread, the entire nation was indignant. Now, all the representatives have returned to the country and arrived in Shanghai. The reporter from Guoguang News Agency interviewed Mr. Shen Yugong, a veteran Lianghua team member and World Games representative, at Mr. Delin's residence. He explained the reasons for our basketball team's failure in the tournament as follows:

Mr. Shen stated that regarding the reasons for our basketball team's disastrous defeat, the old arguments of not having recovered physical strength and being nervous were certainly factors. However, the most important reason is that Mr. Dong (Shouyi) should be responsible. This is because when Mr. Dong was training at Qinghua, he taught new rules, such as that after a free throw is made, there is no need to go to the center line to jump ball, taking two steps counts as a foul, and he mostly practiced the new ten-second rule. Unexpectedly, this time they were still using the old rules from before 1934. So, when we arrived there, what we had learned was not applicable, and we rushed to change our methods, but our hands and feet were not coordinated, and we were out of sync. When the competition day arrived at the tournament, Mr. Dong fell ill, truly ill. Although he also had the desire to win, he had expressed before the game that he would go onto the court despite his illness. Later, the hospital warned him that if he went out and something dangerous happened, they would not be responsible. Finally, Mr. Dong panicked and called Mr. Li An to entrust him with many on-the-spot strategies. However, what Mr. Dong had in mind was completely different from the situation during the game, so Mr. Li was also unable to cope. This is because he had to follow Mr. Dong's instructions and could not make decisions casually. For example, Mr. Dong instructed him when to substitute players, but when Mr. Li arrived, he saw that they were not allowed to substitute players. Even if it was necessary to substitute, he could not put them in. Also, there was a limit of at most seven players entering the court, so he also panicked and was unable to take measures. You see, the instructor is the commander of an army, but now there is a lack of command, and the players on the spot naturally have more concerns. How could they not lose?

In short, we have failed and let down the country's trust. However, looking back at the situation at the time, there are some regrets. That is, our country lacks organization.

Before the World Games basketball tournament began, the Japanese players saw our skills during practice. They even asked the tournament authorities to change the order of the games, wanting to avoid meeting our country in the preliminary round. However, we didn't know this until the game was about to start. We only learned about the Japanese request later. At that time, who didn't predict that we would win?

As for the skills of the American team, their tall stature certainly gave them a lot of advantages. However, their coach was also incomparable to ours. They could lose in the first half, but they could always win in the second half. This is the power of guidance. Because their guidance only requires a simple signal, and the whole team is like a completely different team. All the strategies follow the coach's intentions. As for their passes, they never fall into the hands of others. Furthermore, with their tall stature, the ball is still in their hands. Even when they are in dire straits, they have a tactic, which is to pass from afar, with the center standing in a suitable position and able to score with two steps. However, they are unwilling to do this.

Later, when the reporter asked about the situation of the Tianjin Lianghua team, he said that the veteran Lianghua team members are now running around for food and clothing. Therefore, it will probably not be easy to form a strong Lianghua team in the future. Logically speaking, the strength of a group requires taking care of the lives of its members and keeping them together permanently, which is impossible. Therefore, I also hope that the government will come forward to organize a national team, actively train them, and hope to compete in the next World Games.

Finally, he said that he would stay in Shanghai for one or two more days and then go north to Tianjin on the seventh. As for Xu Zhaoxiong, because his home is in Shanghai, he will not go to Tianjin for the time being.

Reflections on Participating in the World Games and Traveling in Europe: The Rebirth of Germany (1)

— Li Huitang

As the English proverb says, "Heaven helps those who help themselves." The German spirit of self-governance is deeply understood by both men and women. In a great occasion, they divide the work and cooperate, but do not rely on others. Even between men and women, there is no habit of excessive politeness. In the car, young women rarely give up their seats, except for the elderly or those with disabilities. Everyone goes their own way, without paying attention to others, nor expecting others to pay attention to them. In middle- and lower-class families, they never dream of having servants. The housewife always takes care of the housework herself. Even in wealthy families, there are very few employees. Occupations in society are also distributed very evenly. It is said that women who are married and have husbands to support them are not allowed to look for jobs again, so as not to block the opportunities of others. Therefore, there are very few unemployed workers in Germany. In short, their—especially the women's—spirit of self-governance is truly admirable.

(7) Promotion and Reward of Sports

The health of the German nation, the robustness of both men and women, is largely due to the great gains made by the government and society in promoting sports. Sports venues are everywhere in any city, and places for rest and recreation are also well considered. Like Berlin, a city with millions of people, the land is worth its weight in gold, but in the middle of the city, there is a vast and lush park. It is said that physical education has begun to be compulsory in elementary schools, and it has become a required subject in middle schools and universities. The German tradition of fencing has not yet disappeared. We often see strong men with scars on their faces on the road. The number of scars is a sign of the depth of experience. The more scars, the more respected they are by women. They love heroes and athletes, which is something that other countries cannot match. Like the acrobatic boxing master "Smith," the whole country treats him as a national hero and loves him. Even the leader Hitler personally encouraged and praised him. Also, the winner of the modern pentathlon at this conference was a German officer. The day after he won, he was promoted two ranks. Who wouldn't want to work hard to sow good seeds and cultivate them carefully, hoping for the same harvest in the future? Who wouldn't want to put in special effort in the way of sports? It is said that in recent years, the government and society have established standards for various sports. Anyone who can reach or exceed those standards will be awarded medals or certificates according to their performance. People with considerable skill can test themselves anytime and anywhere. This is truly an excellent way to promote and reward. This is why Germany has achieved excellent results in the conference. A certain sports magazine said it well, "The progress of sports depends on the cultivation and growth in ordinary times, and it goes hand in hand with culture. One or two days of training is in vain." "Athletic progress is from growth and culture, and not from mere training." Our country always digs a well when thirsty and plays the trick of helping seedlings grow by pulling them up. How can we compare to others?

(8) Uniform Commodity Prices

When we first went to Germany to buy souvenirs, we wanted to be careful and inquired about the prices of goods everywhere, but we ran an infinite amount of unnecessary errands. It turned out that all local or foreign goods in Germany have been reviewed by the General Chamber of Commerce, and the prices are uniform and unchangeable. No matter if you go from the east side of the city to the west side, you will never find a slightly cheaper price for the same item. If someone privately sells goods at a lower price, the government will severely punish them if they find out. However, there are still Jewish shops where you can get a discount if you are introduced by an acquaintance. This kind of activity is a secret within a secret and cannot be made known to others. Germany's recent exclusion of Jews is probably one of the reasons for this. Uniform commodity prices can eliminate the evils of unscrupulous merchants monopolizing, defrauding, and deceiving. It is indeed beneficial to society and the people. I hope that our country's chambers of commerce will also rise up and follow suit. Although our country is vast and rich in resources, and it may be a bit difficult to do, if the chambers of commerce in various places cooperate without fear of trouble, there will be a day when it can be done.

The above eight points are the facts that I know in more detail and are worthy of learning from. Other things such as the magnificent construction (all scientific), the might of the military and police, and the convenience of transportation (just in Berlin, there are trains, long-distance buses, trams, subways, elevated trains, airships, and airplanes. Just trams alone, there are more than 170 routes in the city, and nearly 300,000 cars) are all things that Germans can be proud of. I am not bragging for them, but the facts tell us that our country looks uglier in comparison. Although I love my country as much as anyone else, I dare not argue for it or conceal it, cover up my conscience, and bury the good things of others. However, things are done by people. Today's Germany was not created or given by God. It is the good fruit obtained through its own struggle and striving. Since we are all human beings, what others can succeed in, why should we be afraid? May my compatriots work together with one heart and rise up to fight, and strive to catch up.

2,000-Meter Race: New World Record

Created by a Hungarian Athlete

Havas, 4th, Hungarian Capital: A 2,000-meter race was held here. The champion was Hungarian athlete Szabo, who broke the world record with a time of 5 minutes and 20.4 seconds. The old record of 5 minutes and 21.8 seconds was held by the famous French professional athlete Ladoumegue.

Municipal National Arts Hall to Hold National Arts Lecture

In order to integrate national arts with theory, the Shanghai Municipal National Arts Hall is holding a national arts lecture and inviting famous national arts figures to serve as lecturers in turn. Yesterday morning (the 4th), Tang Hao, the former director of the Editorial Department of the Central National Arts Hall, was invited to give a lecture, and Wu Changyi, a shorthand teacher at the China Vocational Supplementary School, was asked to record it. The topic was Martial Dance and Martial Arts. The lecture was detailed and the understanding was clear. More than 100 people from various national arts organizations in the city and members of the hall attended. Ministry of Education Advisor Gu Zhaolin's Report on Inspecting Education in Shandong Province

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the Shandong Provincial Department of Education on the 3rd, stating: According to the report on inspecting education in Shandong Province submitted to the Ministry by Gu Zhaolin, Advisor of the Ministry, the department has achieved considerable success in handling compulsory education, and deserves commendation. In addition, there are many commendable aspects regarding various other educational endeavors. Now, the inspection opinions submitted are copied and issued separately. You are hereby instructed to comply with them and report back. This order includes a copy of the inspection opinions as follows:

(1) At the beginning of the establishment of provincial short-term elementary schools, the department took overall responsibility for the situation, assigning personnel to various districts to oversee the implementation. As a result, they were established on schedule, with consistent methods, meticulous planning, and thorough preparation, demonstrating great effort. However, due to the urgency of time, the training period for teachers was somewhat short and should be extended slightly during the next training session.

(2) The short-term elementary schools in the counties inspected, such as Qingcheng, Qidong, Linzi, Yidu, Weixian, Huangxian, Penglai, and Pingyuan, were filled with students, teachers were working diligently, the format was orderly, and the spirit was invigorated. Overall, they have achieved considerable results and are highly commendable.

(3) The department's method of establishing a local elementary school communication network centered on the fifth section of each county has been effective in conveying government orders, introducing knowledge, and promoting communication. However, the scope of material for the elementary school communication network and the "Basic Education Monthly" should be expanded and enriched.

(4) The academic performance of general short-term elementary school students is comparable to that of students completing the second grade of regular elementary school. Those who are slightly older are comparable to the upper semester of the third grade of regular elementary school. If they can continue for one year, they can roughly equal the graduation level of regular elementary school. The department already had a plan to select some short-term elementary schools to extend for one year, which should be approved for pilot implementation. According to the Henan Provincial Kaifeng Education Experimental Zone, the experiment of completing the four-year curriculum of regular elementary school in two and a half years has already achieved results. However, the age of admission is still based on the school age of elementary school. The school age of short-term elementary schools is higher, so it is more likely to complete the four-year curriculum of regular elementary school in two years. If successful in the future, changing rural regular elementary schools to short-term elementary schools will increase their effectiveness many times over.

(5) According to the actual situation in the whole province, there are only two ways to expand short-term compulsory education: one is to retain the original school foundation and continue to operate, and the other is to establish new schools in locations where schools have not been established. According to the current situation, there is a feeling of average distribution, with a slight tendency to be scattered. Although the "Elementary School Communication Network" is implemented to the greatest extent, it is difficult to completely remedy the situation. The local conditions should be considered. In the moderate locations of the townships, where the school foundation is better and there are more out-of-school children, the number of grades should be increased. It is not necessary to limit one class per school. The principals should be selected from those with proven results, in order to establish the center of the short-term elementary school and achieve the practical results of communication and unity.

(6) In general short-term elementary schools, there are more female students. In the counties of Jiaodong, almost all are female students, and male students are almost non-existent. Among the female students, there must be many who are older and need training in household affairs. In the next selection of teachers, female teachers who are from the local area, physically strong, and qualified should also be employed to facilitate practical needs.

(7) Since Changshan Islands are a special zone and are not subordinate to Penglai, short-term elementary schools should be established there. The department should decide the number of schools to be established based on the dispersed residence of the islanders, or compare it to counties of the same population and divide them into cases. The department should decide how to handle this.

(8) Yang Chengrong, the magistrate of Qingcheng County, has not been in office for long, but he has been able to plan in many ways in a poor area. Within a short period of time, he has completely popularized compulsory education in the whole county, which is truly enthusiastic and responsible. He should be commended as an encouragement.

(9) The school buildings and equipment of general elementary schools in the counties of Jiaodong are quite impressive. However, the salaries of teachers are quite uneven, and the teaching methods are also outdated. The department should select a moderate location (Yantai or Weixian), assign a special commissioner to preside over the organization of training classes, seminars, and research meetings to teach practical knowledge of teaching and moral education, and stimulate their interest to change the atmosphere and improve their skills.

(10) The provincial No. 1 Experimental Elementary School, the attached elementary school of the Jinan Women's Normal School, and the Jinan Municipal No. 1 Experimental Elementary School have achieved results in their past experimental work. The future facilities plan is being implemented, and they are generally working diligently with practical research. Other elementary schools that are responsible for experimental work that have not been inspected must also have excellent selections. However, the establishment of experimental elementary schools and attached elementary schools are all responsible for guiding local elementary schools. In addition to general research, it is appropriate to investigate the actual problems of local elementary schools and also serve as the object of research work. For example, the provincial No. 1 Experimental Elementary School has already implemented the guidance of local elementary schools in various counties, so it should first focus on the improvement methods of the complete elementary schools in various counties. The nearby experimental elementary schools and attached elementary schools do not need to study the same problems as that school. For example, the attached elementary school of the Jinan Women's Normal School has a foundation for compiling teaching materials, so other schools do not need to gather together to compile their own teaching materials. They can choose other work to contribute. Currently, the elementary schools in Jinan City and the suburbs are compiling their own teaching materials, which has become a fashion of the time. If they intend to win, the drawbacks of partial and incomplete omissions will be difficult to avoid. Educational problems are very broad, so it is appropriate to correct the wind of general agreement and hope to achieve the effect of division of labor and cooperation.

(11) The two manufacturing plants for instruments and specimens established by the department have not been open for long, but the results are remarkable. Now, the scientific equipment that elementary schools should have does not need to be purchased from Tianjin or Shanghai. In addition, they are cheap and of good quality, and easy to popularize, which is truly commendable. However, the two plants are only set up with 6,000 yuan, and the factory equipment is still largely incomplete and should be expanded at any time.

(12) This year, secondary schools and above are concentrated in the military department, with strict discipline and vigorous spirit, and the handling is quite successful. In addition, they can explain the matters of discipline and service to the students in detail, and sit back and reap the benefits of subtle influence, which is in line with the principles of education and is permissible.

(13) The provincial No. 1 and No. 2 People's Education Guidance Zones are handled with great spirit, and their central undertakings have achieved considerable results. Qu Zhenqian, director of the No. 1 People's Education Guidance Zone, and Yang Yixin, director of the No. 2 People's Education Guidance Zone, are both conscientious and do not avoid hardship. They should be commended as an encouragement.

(14) The Provincial People's Experimental School is located in Jinan City, and due to environmental factors, it has little practical effect. It should be moved to Weixian, where industry is growing, to select a more moderate location and establish contact with factories and society to continue operating.

Meeting of the Electrical Engineering Terminology Review Committee

The Electrical Engineering Terminology Review Committee of the Ministry of Education held a meeting at the National Translation and Compilation Bureau at 9:00 AM on the 4th. Those present included Huang Jianzhong, Director of the Department representing Minister Wang, Chen Kezhong, Director of the National Translation and Compilation Bureau, Yun Zhen (Construction Committee), Chairman of the Committee, Gu Yuxiu (Tsinghua University), Chen Zhang Zhang Jiangshu (Central University), Yang Jianchu (Jinling University), Huang Xiuqing Tao Fengshan (Ministry of Communications), Qiu Weiyu (Jiaotong University), Li Ximou (Jinan University), Yang Xiaoshu (China Science Society), Yang Zhaoyan (Central Research Institute), Kang Qinggui (National Translation and Compilation Bureau), and other members, more than ten people in total. After the ceremony, the review work began at 10:00 AM. The electrical engineering terminology is divided into four parts: general, power, telecommunications, and electrochemistry, with a total of over 10,000 terms. Since last year, the Translation and Compilation Bureau has been collecting materials. The first draft was completed last summer and was sent by the bureau to the engineering colleges of universities across the country, various factories, the Chinese Institute of Engineers, and the Chinese Institute of Electrical Engineers for review by experts jointly recommended. The committees in Shanghai have held meetings more than ten times. This is the final review. It is said that each committee member needs to hold meetings daily due to their official duties, and it will take several days to complete. After the terminology is decided by the review committee, it will be submitted to the Ministry of Education for promulgation and implementation.

Director of the East Asia Bureau of the Japanese Foreign Ministry, Kuwashima, Arrived in Shanghai from Japan Yesterday to Go to Beijing and Convey New Instructions to Kawagoe

Kuwashima, Director of the East Asia Bureau of the Japanese Foreign Ministry, who was specially sent to China to meet with Ambassador Kawagoe and convey new instructions, arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 3:20 PM on the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru, accompanied by Secretary Tanoue. He then held consultations at the Consulate General with Vice Admiral Sato, Naval Attache of the Embassy, Major General Kitadoshi, Military Attache, Wakasugi, Councilor and Consul General in Shanghai, Tajiri, and Yoshioka. At 7:00 PM, Wakasugi and others held a banquet at the Ambassador's residence to welcome him. It is believed that if necessary, he will visit the Chinese authorities to conduct side negotiations. After meeting with Ambassador Kawagoe in Nanjing, his mission will be completed, and he has no hope of meeting with the Chinese side.

Kuwashima's flight to Beijing is expected to last for a considerable amount of time. In addition to assisting Kawagoe in the negotiations, he also plans to visit various important Chinese figures to probe the attitude of the Chinese side.

Shallow Water in Hunan Interrupts Navigation

Ships Arrive at Jinggang and Barges Transfer Cargo, Increasing the Barge Fee by 15%

The shipping route from Shanghai to Changsha, Hunan, is served by regular liners operated by five companies: Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Sanbei, China Merchants, and Nisshin. This year, due to the bumper harvest in Hunan Province, the amount of goods going to and from this route is unprecedented in the past 20 years. Food is the main commodity coming from Changsha, and cotton textiles and sundry goods are the main commodities going from Shanghai. The transportation on the Changsha route has been very developed for each company in the past four months. Now, at a time when cargo transportation is supposed to be congested, the Xiang River suddenly reported a sharp drop in water level. At its highest, the water level reached more than 50 feet, but it has been decreasing day by day in the past month. Recently, it has dropped to a few inches above four feet, and navigation has been obstructed. Yesterday, it dropped even further to three feet and eight inches. The Hunan liners of each shipping company have all been blocked because each ship has a draft of more than ten feet for larger ships and six feet even for shallow-water ships. As a result, the Jiangda and Jiangjing ships of the China Merchants Bureau, the Changsha of Taikoo, and the Hongyuan, Hongheng, Hongli, and Hongzhen ships of Sanbei are all unable to reach Changsha from the Xiang River. The navigation route has been interrupted, and cargo transportation has also been hindered. Now, in order to remedy the situation of transportation on the Hunan waterway and to dredge the accumulated goods to and from, each shipping company has decided that each river ship will only open to Jinggang, and then each shipping company will send small motorboats and flat-bottomed barges to Jinggang to pick up and transfer the goods to Changsha. At the same time, goods from Hunan will also be barged to Jinggang and transferred to ships. In addition, starting tomorrow, the shallow-water lotus fee will be increased by 15% across the board, and the Hunan-Changsha route will be maintained with great effort.

British Taikoo Company Resumes Operations of Suspended Ships

Heavy Cargo to Nanhua, Taking the Opportunity to Ship Three Ships First

The Nanhua route of the British Taikoo Company is its main route. It has more than 20 regular and irregular ships operating between Shanghai, Shantou, Hong Kong, Xiamen, Guangdong, and also calling at various ports in North China. Before the past half year, due to the decline in cargo transportation and the fact that the shipping in North China was exclusively dominated by Japan, the company's coastal shipping line was severely affected. At that time, it announced the suspension of seven ships on the Nanhua route to reduce losses. Since the unification of the two Guangdong provinces and the abolition of the special tax collected by Chen Jitang, the economy of the two Guangdong provinces has been revived, and the amount of goods going from Shanghai to Nanhua has greatly increased. The three companies have already agreed to increase the water fees from Shanghai to Nanhua by 15%. Recently, due to the increase in outgoing goods, Taikoo Company is taking advantage of this opportunity to resume the operation of the seven ships that have been suspended for half a year. In the past two days, it has first resumed the shipping of the Suiyang and Ganzhou ships to Nanhua to transport goods from Shanghai. Today, it has sent the Chongqing ship to resume service. The other four ships are also in the process of planning and arranging schedules. Once determined, all ships will resume operations.

Zou Bingwen and Others Organize Cotton Industry Economic Research Association, Zou Appointed as Chairman, Ye Yuanding and Others as Executive Directors, Local Representatives to Be Established in All Cotton-Producing Provinces

Cotton industry figures Zou Bingwen, Ye Yuanding, Li Shengbo, and others, for the purpose of studying cotton industry economic issues, improving the cotton industry, and developing the national economy, have organized the Chinese Cotton Industry Economic Research Association, which has already been established. Zou Bingwen has been elected as Chairman. The details are recorded below:

Article 1 of the Association's Articles of Association states that the name of the association is the Chinese Cotton Industry Economic Research Association. Article 2 states that the purpose of the association is to connect comrades, study cotton industry economic issues, thereby improving the cotton industry and developing the national economy. Article 3 states that the association's activities are tentatively defined as follows: (1) to study various cotton industry issues, (2) to investigate the domestic and international cotton industry situation, (3) to compile and translate cotton industry books and newspapers, (4) to propose and deliberate on matters concerning the improvement of the cotton industry economy. Article 4 states that the association's membership is divided into the following four types: (1) Basic members: those who currently serve in cotton industry organizations, have considerable research or experience in the cotton industry economy, and are willing to join, are basic members of the association. (2) Ordinary members: those who are interested in studying the cotton industry economy and are introduced by two or more basic members may become ordinary members of the association. (3) Group members: public and private organizations related to the cotton industry that support the association's purpose and assist the association in its activities may become group members of the association. (4) Supporting members: those who support the association's activities or donate funds to the association may become supporting members of the association. Article 5 states that the association's headquarters are temporarily located at Room 610, 6th Floor, 113 Jiujiang Road, Shanghai. Article 6 states that the association shall have nine to eleven directors, who shall be elected by a general meeting of members to form a board of directors. The board of directors shall mutually elect one chairman and two executive directors to manage the association's daily affairs. Article 7 states that the association shall have one secretary-general and several local representatives to manage the association's affairs in various regions. The association shall have several staff members to handle editing, accounting, and documentation, and may appoint several advisors if necessary, all of whom shall be appointed by the board of directors. Article 8 states that the term of office for the chairman, executive directors, and directors shall be two years, and they may be re-elected for consecutive terms upon expiration. Article 9 states that the association shall hold a board meeting every six months to discuss the progress of association affairs, which shall be convened by the chairman. An annual meeting shall be held every year, and the location and date shall be determined by the board of directors. Article 10 states that the association's membership fees are stipulated as follows: (1) Admission fee: Members shall pay an admission fee of 50 cents when joining. (2) Annual membership fee: Members shall pay an annual membership fee of 50 cents each year. (3) Group membership fee: Group members shall voluntarily donate at least 20 yuan or more. Article 11 states that the association's regular expenses shall be maintained by membership fees in principle, and if it is necessary to carry out activities, the board of directors shall decide to raise funds. Article 12 states that if it is necessary to amend the association's constitution, it shall be amended by a general meeting of members upon the proposal of more than one-quarter of the members. Article 13 states that the association's rules of procedure shall be formulated separately. Article 14 states that these articles of association shall come into effect from the date of approval by the general meeting of members.

Directors and Representatives: The directors of the association are Zou Bingwen, Ye Yuanding, Ma Guangwen, Jiang Hanluo, Sun Yushu, Ni Jing, Li Shengbo, Qu Guojuan, Tu Xunxian, Feng Zefang, Zhou Yousheng, and eleven others. Zou Bingwen was elected as Chairman, and Li Shengbo and Ye Yuanding were elected as Executive Directors. The Secretary-General is concurrently held by Executive Director Ye. Local representatives: (1) Anhui: Duan Tianjue, (2) Jiangxi: Liao Xianyang, (3) Hunan: Zhou Gan, (4) Hubei: Jiang Hanluo, Zhang Jingyun, Liu Qin'an, (5) Shandong: Zhou Shisheng, Zhang Zongren, Liu Xin, (6) Gansu: Ji Yun, (7) Shaanxi: Tu Xunxian, Zhang Yun (8) Hunan: Qu Guojuan, Guo Xingze, (9) Zhejiang: Xiao Fu, (10) Shanxi: Mu Wanglun, (11) Hebei: Sun Yushu, (12) Jiangsu: Ni Keding, Tang Dongshan, (13) Shanghai: Ma Guangwen. The association's Shanghai office is located in the Central Cotton Adulteration and Mixing Prohibition Office of the National Economic Council's Cotton Control Committee.

At about 9:30 yesterday morning, two platoons of Japanese troops, about sixty or seventy people, all carrying long guns, marched from the Japanese Marine Corps headquarters on Jiangwan Road, across the Tiantong'an railway tracks, through the Dongbinshan Road intersection, and Tongji Road, and marched into the open space at the end of Huayuan Street and the Tanwu Shipyard behind the 63rd Garden. Also, at about 9:00 yesterday morning, six or seven hundred Japanese soldiers were conducting drills in Hongkou Garden. However, this is a common occurrence. Before the Japanese sailor incident on the 23rd of last month, Japanese troops often conducted drills there.
