Japanese and British Coal Compete Fiercely, Seeking to Dominate Our Coal Industry Market, Domestic Coal Sales Account for Only One-Tenth, Due to Weak Capital and High Transportation Costs

The dumping of Japanese coal in China is managed by the Mitsui and Mitsubishi trading companies. Their sales base is in major commercial ports such as Shanghai, Tianjin, Hankou, Qingdao, and Hong Kong. The sales method in the interior is managed by Chinese agents. Therefore, China's coal market is almost in the hands of the Japanese. However, in Shanghai, Australian coal used to have the greatest sales power, but recently, it has also changed greatly, and Fushun coal mined by Japanese merchants has taken the lead. Kailuan coal has been overwhelmed by Fushun coal. The coal mine areas in various parts of North China are mostly mined by foreigners. For example, Kailuan Coal Mine is mined by British merchants, and dozens of major coal mines in Shandong's Fangzi, Yinzhen, Zibo, Jilin's Majiagou and Shisonggang, and Liaoning's Benxi, Fushun, Yantai, and Liaoyang are mined by Japanese merchants. Because the Chinese have weak capital and a harsh environment, the production and market share of the Jingxing, Lincheng, Shimensai, Tongshan, Jiawang, Cixian, Wanping, Pingshan, and Changxing coal mines they have mined have fallen behind. Currently, Fushun coal and other Japanese coal are being dumped heavily in Shanghai. Although British merchants' Kailuan coal is competing with it, Chinese coal is unable to compete. Therefore, it is estimated that Japanese coal such as Fushun accounts for 70% of coal sales in Shanghai, Kailuan coal accounts for 20%, and Chinese coal accounts for only 10%. The reason why Chinese coal cannot compete with Japanese and British coal is that transportation costs are expensive and costs are higher. Therefore, the North China coal market is dominated by Japan, and the coal markets in the provinces along the Yangtze River and the provinces of Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong are being competed for by Japanese and British coal. Although the Shanghai Coal Industry Trade Association has a strong patriotic enthusiasm and is actively promoting it, it is unable to do so due to the environment, and the coal production in our country is being manipulated by foreigners, which is a cause for concern.

Fierce Competition in Sino-European Shipping, Foreign Merchants' Pooling Alliance Breaks Down, Netherlands to Build Three Giant Ships After Japan

Shanghai Times News Agency reports that the issue of Sino-European shipping is not only a struggle between Britain, Germany, and Japan, but also involves the participation of the Netherlands.

There are more than 400 ships

from various countries belonging to the shipping companies of various countries in Shanghai. At first, they competed for their strengths and competed with each other. Since the implementation of the pooling system, the foreign shipping companies have reluctantly reached an agreement. For the shipment of goods, ships are evenly distributed according to the pooling points. After the implementation of this measure, the German North German Lloyd shipping company's monthly dispatch was reduced from three ships to the current one ship per month, which was the most affected. The company expressed its opposition, but was constrained by other companies and failed.

Recently, the Japanese

International Steamship Company suddenly built a giant ship and joined the Sino-European shipping competition. (The two ships that have sailed before are the Xiangteng Maru and the Yizhi Maru.) It has now decided to build two 10,000-ton giant ships with a speed of 20 nautical miles per hour, which can be added successively within the year, and intends to compete with other countries' postal ships with low water freight. After the announcement of this measure, other shipping companies were quite uneasy. For the sake of competition, merchants such as Germany and Britain have risen up to build ships, and the Shanghai Foreign Merchants' Cargo Pooling Alliance has suddenly broken down.

The Dutch Shipping

Company is now following in the footsteps of Japanese merchants and building three giant ships. Two of them are larger, with a tonnage of 16,000 tons, and one is smaller with a tonnage of 10,000 tons. The speed is 19 nautical miles to 21.5 nautical miles per hour. It is heard that the larger one is being built in Hamburg, Germany, and one is being built in the Netherlands. It is expected to arrive in the Far East in May next year. From then on, there will be another strong enemy in Sino-European shipping.

Moreover, the long-distance travel from Shanghai to Chengdu only takes eight hours to arrive.

Ways to Reorganize Feikesi Marconi's Debt

Interest to Be Paid Semi-Annually from July, Principal to Be Repaid from June in 30 Years, All Amounts to Be Paid Off in 64 Years

The Ministry of Finance announced the following measures today (6th) to reorganize Feikesi Marconi's debts. The Ministry of Finance announced the following measures to reorganize Feikesi Marconi's debts. The Chinese government signed a contract with Marconi Wireless Electric Machine Co., Ltd. on August 27, 1918, for a loan of 600,000 pounds in English gold with an 8% ten-year term, and the 8% ten-year term English gold loan of 1,803,200 pounds borrowed from Feikesi Co., Ltd. on October 1, 1919. The reorganization measures have been formulated, and are hereby announced as follows: (1) Interest: From July 1, 1936, interest will be paid at a rate of 1.5% per week for the first year, and will be increased by 0.25% per year thereafter, until it increases to 3% per week in 1942. Thereafter, the rate will be uniformly 3% per week until the treasury bonds are paid off. Interest will be paid twice a year on June 30 and December 31. (2) Repayment of principal: From June 30, 1941, 1% will be repaid each year for the first three years, 3% will be repaid each year for the next four years, 2.5% will be repaid each year for the next eight years, 3% will be repaid each year for the next eleven years, and 4% will be repaid each year for the last nine years. All amounts will be paid off in 1975. Starting from 1941, a lottery will be held once in March each year. The government may increase the amount of repayment before any repayment period with sufficient notice, without adding any additional fees. (3) Repayment of principal and interest: The Chinese government's salt tax revenue, excluding the amount that has been designated as loan collateral and mortgage, will be used as collateral. (4) All accrued interest before June 30, 1936, will be waived.

County Land Value Tax Issue Closes Yesterday, Decision to Levy This Month, County Magistrate Li Goes to Province to Report

Li Zhifu, the magistrate of Shanghai County, convened local gentry and leaders from various districts to discuss their opinions on the pilot land value tax at the Daquanfu Restaurant on Zhaojiabang Road yesterday (5th) at noon. The attendees included Qin Yanqi, Tang Fuyin, Shi Ansheng, Yao Huibo, Zhang Fengshan, Peng Yintian, Zhang Jingye, Wu Jingqing, Shi Yangyong, Zhao Qianli, Ge Xiusheng, Xing Zhigang, Wu Shifang, Chen Pinyi, Zhang Wuwu, and 18 others. First, County Magistrate Li reported on the important points of the provincial order to pilot the land value tax and the county's preparations for collecting the land value tax. Then, Wu Shifang, Zhang Fengshan, Ge Xiusheng, Xing Zhigang, and Zhao Qianli reported on the wishes of the people in each district and their opinions on the land value tax. Zhang Fengshan suggested that local people should support the implementation of the land value tax in order to complete local autonomy. The total county tax revenue should not be less than in the past, but the benefits that landowners derive from the land should be sufficient to pay the land tax. The fairness and accuracy of the standard price should be ensured, and adjustments should be made in a timely manner to meet the needs of the situation. Then, Qin Yanqi, Shi Ansheng, Yao Huiquan, Wu Jingqing, Shi Yangyong, and others expressed their opinions. County Magistrate Li also explained the laws and regulations and expressed his opinions after the gentry expressed their opinions. The general points were: (1) to maintain the safety of the revenue budget, (2) to not increase the burden on rural land, and (3) to moderately adjust the tax rate. After joint discussion, it was agreed that the land value tax is one of the land policies set by Dr. Sun Yat-sen, and the county should be the first to pilot it this year. The county government will collect it on schedule, and will examine the actual situation. When the second phase of the tax is opened, the standard land price and tax rate will be adjusted to ensure fairness and accuracy. The people and the government will all benefit from the actual benefits. The county magistrate and the local leaders all believed that a satisfactory result had been achieved, so they held a dinner party. County Magistrate Li also hoped that local leaders would persuade the various households to pay taxes on time. However, although the tax collection documents have been rushed, they are still far from being completed. The opening date of the tax will definitely be delayed for a few days. County Magistrate Li returned to the county government to handle everything after the banquet, and went to the province last night to report everything to Chairman Chen and Finance Director Chen.

Central Bank Cancels Fictitious Price, French Franc Exchange Rate Temporarily Stabilizes, 630 French Francs Equal 100 National Currency, Unless There Are Other Changes, It Will Not Fall Again

After the French government implemented a new monetary policy to prevent capital outflow and devalued the French franc, international exchange rates changed drastically. Various countries are seeking ways to deal with it separately, and our country's exchange rate against the French franc has also been affected. The Central Bank's foreign exchange listing has been set at a fictitious price of 582 French francs per 100 National Currency since the 28th of last month. Afterwards, it continued to fall, falling to 620 French francs per 100 National Currency last Saturday (3rd), but it was still a fictitious price. Now the French government's French franc devaluation policy has been successful. It is scheduled to reduce tariffs from October 10, and reduce the surtax on our country's imported goods from 15% to 10%. Other countries have also cancelled the surtax. This move aims to realize its free trade policy and has no impact on us. However, according to a reporter from Xin Xin News Agency, at 10:00 a.m. on the 5th, the Central Bank's foreign exchange listing was 630 French francs per 100 National Currency, which was 10 French francs lower than last Saturday. Compared with the 464 French francs per 100 National Currency before the French franc devaluation, the difference is a huge 166 French francs. The "fictitious price" has been cancelled. According to the financial community, if the French government does not take other actions, the current price of the French franc can be temporarily stabilized and will not fall again. The exchange rates of London, New York, Berlin, Japan, Hong Kong, etc. are still normal and have not changed.

Postal 40th Anniversary Commemorative Stamps

To Be Issued from October 10, Divided into Four Types, Including a Commemorative Album

The Directorate General of Posts of the Ministry of Communications issued an order stating that this year marks the 40th anniversary of the opening of the postal service in our country. In order to commemorate this occasion, the Directorate General of Posts has presented it to the Ministry of Communications for approval to issue commemorative stamps for the 40th anniversary of the opening of the postal service, divided into four types: 2 cents, 5 cents, 25 cents, and 1 yuan. Each type has a different design. It is scheduled to be sold at various post offices from October 10, 1936. When the public purchases them, they can also apply for them to be canceled with the post office date stamp. In order to facilitate collectors to collect them, a commemorative stamp album for the 40th anniversary of the opening of the postal service has been specially printed. It will be sold simultaneously by major post offices. This commemorative stamp album comes with a set of commemorative stamps, which are sold at the face value of the stamps (i.e., 1 yuan, 3 jiao, and 2 fen) and no additional fees will be charged. If you want to paste the stamps in the test album and apply for them to be canceled with the date stamp, you can also do so. The sale of the above commemorative stamps and stamp albums is limited to the end of March 1937. The sale will be stopped after the deadline, but they can still be used to pay postage. From July 1, 1937, they will be abolished and will not be allowed to be used. However, the public who hold these stamps will still be allowed to exchange them for ordinary stamps of the same value at various post offices every month (i.e., from July 1, 1937 to September 30, 1937). This is to inform Director Zha Peilin of the Bureau, September 30.

Method for Sending Parcels to Yugoslavia

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1358 states: According to International Postal Union Circular No. 55441261 of July 30th of this year, in response to a letter from the Yugoslavian Postal Service, in accordance with their customs regulations and to facilitate customs procedures, you are requested to circulate a notice to the postal services of all countries, informing senders that for parcels sent to Yugoslavia, the invoice should be signed and sent separately to the recipient, and the recipient should be notified that a parcel has been sent so that they can present it to customs for inspection when claiming the parcel. This will facilitate customs procedures and serve as a basis for estimating taxes on ordinary or luxury goods. However, the invoice, parcel dispatch note, and tax declaration form, which should arrive with the parcel, should still be handled as usual. A corresponding letter has been issued for review and compliance. This notice is hereby issued for general knowledge. Director Zha Peilin, October 3rd.

Superior Trial Planting of White Cottonseeds

Improvement Association Actively Promotes

The Zhuanqiao Township Rural Improvement Association previously purchased Jiangyin White Cottonseed cottonseeds and distributed them to members for trial planting. The results showed that Jiangyin White Cottonseed is well suited to the local soil. The resulting cotton bolls are not only abundant but also have thin shells, large cotton fibers, long fibers, small cottonseeds, bright white color, and a high lint percentage. Currently, each mu (unit of area) has yielded about two bales. If the weather remains sunny, each mu can yield more than three bales. Shen Xin No. 2 and No. 5 Factories Prepare to Resume Production

Syndicated Loan Not Yet Secured - Work to Begin After Agreement

Shen Xin Textile Company's Yichang Road No. 2 Factory and Huade Road No. 5 Factory, which have been closed, originally planned to resume operations simultaneously when the new cotton season began this year. However, the two factories remain closed to date. According to a reporter from Dagongshe, the main reason for the failure to resume operations is that the issue of financial assistance from the financial community has not yet been properly discussed. Rong Zongjing is struggling to maintain the operations of Factories No. 1, 6, 7, and 9 in the face of sluggish yarn sales. In reality, he has no capacity to raise substantial funds for Factories No. 2 and 5. However, due to the substantial foreign debts of the two factories in the past, the property collateral has become a problem. Although repeated discussions have been held to resume operations, a concrete plan for syndicated assistance has not yet been finalized. Both parties are continuing to negotiate everything and have found a way forward. The two factories can only schedule a start date once all issues have been negotiated and resolved and the syndicate is formally established and loans are issued.

The Central Party Headquarters has begun collecting income tax donations from the salaries and remunerations of public officials from the 1st of this month. The original text of the notice reads: "It has been determined that the government has clearly ordered the collection of income tax from the salaries and remunerations of public officials in the second category of the Provisional Income Tax Regulations, starting from October 1st of this year. The collection of income donations from public officials by the Central Headquarters should cease as of September 30th of this year. All income donations collected by various agencies before October should be submitted to this office for inspection and collection as soon as possible to complete the procedures and conclude. This notice is hereby issued in addition to separate letters. Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang."

Huang Butian Sues Zhu Ziyun - Confirming Biological Mother-Daughter Relationship - Willing to Undergo Blood Type Testing with Zhu and Her Daughter - Court Orders Zhu Ziyun to be Summoned for Further Interrogation

Huang Butian, daughter of the late famous national physician Huang Xiaochu, previously filed a complaint with the Mediation Office of the Special First Court, suing throat specialist and national physician Zhu Ziyun, requesting confirmation that the girl Zhu Amao, raised by Zhu, was born to her and Zhu. The mediation failed, as reported in this newspaper. Huang then retained lawyer Sha Xunxi to formally file a lawsuit against Zhu Ziyun and Zhu Amao to confirm their biological mother-daughter relationship and to order them to cease abusing their rights. The facts of the lawsuit are, in brief: The plaintiff was previously married to Shi Xiugang, while Zhu was a disciple of the plaintiff's father, and therefore they were like siblings. Later, after the plaintiff became a widow, Zhu seduced her, and they had a daughter named Amao (also known as Yuejuan, now 23 years old), who was raised by Zhu. Now Zhu is abusing his rights by not allowing Amao to meet with the plaintiff, so she is requesting confirmation of her biological daughter's identity and an order to cease abusing his rights. The order is to send Zhu Ziyun, Zhu Amao, and the plaintiff to the Zhenru Forensic Institute to test their blood types to determine if they are of the same type, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Gui Yu of the Civil Seventh Division of the Special First Court held a hearing. Zhu Ziyun did not appear because he was seeing patients due to illness and retained lawyer Lu Qi to appear in court to defend him and submit a defense statement. The summons for Zhu Amao was not delivered because Zhu Ziyun refused to accept it. According to Zhu Ziyun's defense statement, he absolutely denied having cohabited with the plaintiff Huang Butian. The daughter Xiao Mao (i.e., Amao) born to the plaintiff was not accepted by the plaintiff's husband's family or her mother's family, so she had no place to go. Therefore, the plaintiff's mother ordered Zhu Ziyun to introduce her to a foster family. Zhu introduced her to his mother-in-law, Ms. Ma, who adopted and raised her to adulthood. Last summer, Xiao Mao fell in love with a Mr. Zhang and married him in early winter. Therefore, the plaintiff's claims are all unfounded rumors and baseless gossip. He also refuted the plaintiff for adding the character "Zhu" to her name and, based on legal principles, requested that the plaintiff's lawsuit be dismissed, etc. After the lawyers for both parties presented their facts, Judge Gui ordered that Zhu Ziyun and Zhu Amao be summoned for another interrogation at a later date.

Case of Obstructing Credit Arises After Seizure of Wang BinYan's Property - Zhang Rongpu and Lawyer Lu Xingyuan Sued - For Lu's Newspaper Publication Alleging Wrongdoing by Wang

Shanghai gentleman Wang Dong, also known as Binyan, mortgaged real estate deeded under the British Certificate No. 552, with Chen Bingqian of a major business serving as the intermediary, and Shen Lianfang serving as the guarantor, to borrow 10,000 taels of silver from the Old Guangdong Bank during the Jiazi Qilu War. When the bank called for repayment, Wang claimed that the funds were used to maintain local order and support the military and provide relief to refugees at the time and should be repaid by the government. He ignored the request. Zhang Rongpu, the manager of the bank, retained lawyer Lu Xingyuan to sue him in court, and subsequently, after a three trial judgment, Wang Binyan lost the case. However, there were repeated twists and turns in between. Not until March of this year did the court execute the seizure of the mortgaged property. Lu Xingyuan, the representative lawyer of the bank, published an announcement in the Xinwenbao regarding the mortgage dispute, stating: "The case of this bank suing Wang Binyan and Shen Lianfang for the execution of the mortgage was based on the final judgment of the Supreme Court of March 25, 1935, and the Shanghai District Court was petitioned to execute it. The original date for seizing the mortgaged property for compensation was August 10th of last year. Later, for some unknown reason, changes occurred and the matter was suspended. After this bank repeatedly petitioned the Judicial Yuan, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the Supreme Court, and the Jiangsu Higher Court to order the Shanghai District Court to expedite enforcement in accordance with the law, after months of delay, the court scheduled the seizure of Wang Binyan's mortgaged property on the 23rd of this month. Unexpectedly, someone claiming to be the 'Zhabei All Circles Relief Association for Wang Binyan Suffering for Public Affairs' convened a meeting without understanding the truth and issued a telegram, intending to overturn the final judgment of the court and delay execution by illegal means, which is quite surprising. The Supreme Court ruled that Wang Binyan's contract with the Governor of Jiangsu Province and Commissioner for Military Rehabilitation in 1914 was after the establishment of the loan agreement, so the claim that the loan was for maintaining local order and raising military expenses is actually an attempt to imply something else. We are afraid that all circles will not understand the truth and misunderstand, so we have entrusted your lawyer to publish this announcement on behalf of us to clarify the truth." Wang Binyan, upon seeing this announcement, believed that the words "attempt to imply something else" were relevant to his reputation and also published an announcement in the Minbao, stating that the total funds advanced by the three groups in those days amounted to 472,312.20 yuan. If it is said that the funds advanced by Binyan were an insinuation, then wouldn't the funds advanced by the other groups also be insinuations? He hoped that the bank would correct the announcement it had published or stop publishing it. Seeing that it continued to be published, Wang wrote a letter of inquiry, stating, "Please provide evidence that the loan was not used to maintain local order and raise military expenses and announce it to the world so that Binyan cannot escape the crime of deceiving the government and deceiving society. Otherwise, all the consequences of the inability to clear the loans borrowed at that time for maintaining local order and raising military expenses, or the government's wavering commitment to repay, and all losses to Binyan's reputation and property shall be borne by your bank. I hope you will understand and reply clearly." Since no satisfactory response has been received to date, Wang has now retained lawyers Tu Zhengugao and Shuo to file a criminal self-accusation against Zhang Rongpu of the bank and lawyer Lu Xingyuan, who published the announcement on his behalf, with the First Special District District Court, detailing the facts of the defendant spreading rumors and obstructing his reputation and credit, requesting punishment according to the law, and also attaching a civil lawsuit requesting compensation for his Jiazi military advances of 228,649.70 yuan, because the government has refused to return them after the defendant published the announcement. He also requested compensation for his personal economic losses of 5,000 yuan per year, calculated over ten years, for a total of 50,000 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Dai Rongduo held a hearing. The plaintiff Wang Binyan did not appear in person, and the defendant Zhang Rongpu also did not surrender himself. Only Lu Xingyuan appeared in court. First, he submitted a counterclaim for false accusation, and then he detailed the procedures of his handling of the lawsuit against Wang Binyan and others for failing to redeem the mortgage on behalf of the bank. Finally, he said that Wang Binyan's lawsuit this time was frivolous, hoping to get rich out of thin air, not hesitating to make an issue out of nothing, and could make me lose face. This kind of atmosphere, I have suffered repeatedly. In fact, people come to court to await the judge's judgment of right and wrong. It cannot be considered a loss of face. If I am found guilty, I will have no regrets even if I am beheaded. If I am innocent, I should ask the court to punish the plaintiff for false accusation. Now that Wang has not appeared in court, I assume he is ashamed to face me. I should ask the court to summon the plaintiff and make a fair judgment. Zhang Rongpu has gone to Hong Kong for business and has nothing to do with him at all. The plaintiff's lawyer then submitted the newspaper to the court and stated that the plaintiff would definitely appear in court and was willing to subpoena Zhang Rongpu. The court then ordered that the hearing be adjourned to the afternoon of the 16th of this month for further interrogation.

Remarried Couple Arrested in Yangtze Hotel - First Wife Went to Wei Ya Where Wedding Had Already Been Held - Police Discovered Location and Arrested Them Late at Night - Judge Advises Both Parties to Seek Reconciliation Out of Court

Liu Guangfa, also known as Buyun, 26 years old, a native of this county, lived in a bungalow at No. 176 Jules Pasteur Road in the French Concession. His family was well-off. On the fourth day of the first lunar month in 1928, he married Chen Lindi (28 years old), also a native of this county, through the introduction of Xu Xinquan and Chen Liangxing. They have been married for nine years and have four children, two of whom have died. There are now one son and one daughter. In January of this year, when Liu worked at the Sino-American Hospital in the French Concession, he met Shen Huizhen (also known as Cizhen, 18 years old), a nurse from Shanghai, who lived at No. 14 Yuanfuli, No. 544 Xinzha Road. In February, Liu changed jobs to the Maichang Hospital on Wuzhou Road, and he and Shen had an affair. Since then, Shen became pregnant, and she is now six or seven months along and will soon give birth. Therefore, they discussed getting married and decided to hold the wedding at the Wei Ya Restaurant on Fuzhou Road on the 4th of this month. On the 3rd of the month, Liu asked his wife Chen for a divorce or separation, but she refused and they parted unhappily. At that time, Liu did not mention that he was going to marry Shen the next day. Liu did not return home that night. Unexpectedly, Chen learned of the wedding and rushed to Wei Ya at about 6:00 PM the day before yesterday. However, the wedding of Liu and Shen had already been completed at 4:00 PM, and all the guests had left. Chen had no choice but to report to the old police station. After investigation by Chinese Detective Li Shugui and Detective Song Wenqing, they learned that Liu and Shen had opened a room at No. 231 Yangtze Hotel as their honeymoon suite. They then went there with French Detective Huo Gengsheng at 2:00 AM and arrested Liu and Shen together. They were taken back to the police station along with a wedding certificate and temporarily detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal First Division of the Special First Court. Criminal Presiding Judge Qian Hongye interrogated them. Lawyer Ru Baozhi of the police station stated the facts and prosecuted them for bigamy under Article 237 of the Criminal Law. Then Chen Lindi identified Liu and asked him, Liu Xianfa, to confess that he had committed bigamy with Shen Huizhen and claimed that he had obtained the consent of his wife Chen and that they had met. Shen Huizhen confessed that she had married Liu, which was true, but she did not know that he already had a wife. Liu also retained lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend him. Judge Qian verified the confessions and ordered both parties to seek reconciliation out of court. He then ordered the case to be adjourned, and Liu and Shen were each granted bail of 300 yuan in cash or a guarantor from a store.

Lixin Accounting School to Offer Income Tax Course

The Income Tax Regulations of our country have been set to be fully implemented starting from January 1st of next year. However, the theory of income tax and the methods of its implementation and calculation are very complex and difficult for the general industry, commerce, and freelance personnel to understand. Lixin Accounting School at No. 406 Jiangxi Road in this city, in view of this, has specially established an Income Tax Crash Course, hoping to enable the managers and accounting personnel of the industrial and commercial sectors and freelance organizations to have a considerable understanding of the various theories of income tax and the methods of its implementation and calculation in a short period of time, so as to avoid various difficulties when it is implemented next year. It is reported that the admission qualifications for the course are: managers, accounting directors, accountants, and freelance personnel from all sectors of industry and commerce can join. The duration of study is ten weeks, with four hours of classes per week. The teaching will be personally undertaken by Dr. Pan Xulun, the principal of the school. Teaching materials are self-compiled, and the tuition fee is eight yuan. Registration starts today, and the starting date is October 21st.

A Mutiny of the Sijiao Mountain Defense Corps: One Soldier Arrested, Li Jilong Hiding in Shanghai, Chongming County Requests Assistance in Apprehension

Sijiao Mountain, located in Zhejiang waters, is under the jurisdiction of the Chongming County government in Jiangsu Province and is designated as the Fifth District. Xu Yunming, a native of Chongming, was appointed district chief by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. Shen Ranya, a native of Qidong, was appointed head of the defense corps by the county government, stationed on the island to protect the residents. In early July of this year, during the handover of district chief and defense corps detachment leaders on the island, for unknown reasons, the Anhui and Shandong factions of the defense corps suddenly mutinied. On the night of July 4th, they killed the district chief and the defense corps detachment leader. They seized thirty-six rifles, more than ten Mauser pistols, and three Browning pistols, extorting three thousand gold pieces from local gentry before fleeing by boat. The Chongming County government, upon receiving the report, ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate. It was discovered that the mutinous soldiers hired a small boat to escape after the incident. En route, they encountered a customs officer's boat passing by. Just as the officer was about to inquire, the soldiers cleverly bound two of their companions at the bow of the boat, falsely claiming that they were escorting captured pirates to Nantong for prosecution. Upon hearing that it was official business, the customs officer did not investigate further, allowing them to escape. When the boat reached Wusong, the soldiers discarded the rifles into the Huangpu River and fled ashore with the Mauser pistols and handguns. Recently, it was discovered that Li Jilong, also known as Li Jilong or Li Xingfu, a 34-year-old native of Jinan, Shandong, was among the mutinous soldiers. His brother resides in Wusong. Li was hiding at his brother's place. The Chongming County Public Security Bureau dispatched detectives to inquire with Li's brother, who revealed that Li was hiding at No. 114 Caishi Road in the French Concession of this city. The detectives, together with detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, requested assistance from the French police the day before yesterday. A detective, Liu Jinrong, was dispatched by the police chief to the address and arrested Li Jilong. He was taken back to the police station. Under interrogation, Li confessed to participating in the mutiny on Sijiao Mountain. He was ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special No. 2 Court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the hearing. Gu Shouxi, a lawyer from the Police Department, presented the case, prosecuting him under Articles 271 and 325 of the Criminal Code. Detective Liu Jinrong reported the process of assisting in the arrest of the defendant. According to Zai Chujun, the leader of the Chongming Public Security Bureau's detective team, who surrendered, requested to be transferred. When questioned, the defendant Li Jilong stated, "At the time, I was playing mahjong when they surrounded me, ordering me to call the detachment leader. The detachment leader walked out with me, and after a dozen steps, they opened fire, killing the detachment leader. When asked how much of the three thousand gold pieces extorted he received, he replied, 'I didn't receive a single cent. It was the Anhui gang who mutinied; I am from Shandong.'" After reviewing the statements, the court ruled that the defendant Li Jilong could be temporarily detained and taken away by the Chongming County detectives, with a three-day deadline to submit official documents for his extradition.

Collapse of a Portuguese-Owned Silver Company Due to Poor Reputation and Slow Business

The Shanghai Jidai Silver Company, located at No. 150 Guangdong Road, was established last April with funding from Portuguese national Remetes and registered at the Portuguese Consulate. Its business activities were ostensibly described as organizing bidding clubs and savings clubs. However, the bidding clubs were essentially the same as lending money at high interest rates, and the savings clubs were a variation of the Wan Guo Sino-French Savings Society. The company's business targeted the hard-earned money of the working class, employing extremely ruthless methods. The Social Affairs Bureau and other agencies were paying close attention, but due to its Portuguese ownership, they were unable to take action. Recently, the company suddenly ceased operations. It is understood that the company suffered from a poor reputation, resulting in very slow business since its opening, and its limited capital was insufficient for turnover. It collapsed a few days ago.

As the report lacked a detailed address, Director Zhang could not make an arrest. He secretly dispatched officers Ye Shouchun and Huang Youfen, a household registration officer, who spent two to three days investigating before finally discovering that the gambling den was located inside No. 61, Maoye Lane. On the evening before last, at around 9 PM, officers Ye and Huang, along with senior police officers, surrounded the front and back doors of the gambling den and arrested twenty-three gamblers inside: Wang Shunfa, Chen San, Wang Wenbin, Hu Axiang, Qiu Heqing, Zhang Awu, Song Wuyan, Chen Wenkui, Wang Agen, Wang Qingxiang, Ye Xing, Zhu Amao, Yang Caibing, Chen Changfa, Sun Fugen, Shao Axun, Lu Guiying, Wang Jinchu, Dong Shunxing, Ye Boying, Han Jinguang, Shu Afa, and Ye Wenyuan, all from Shaoxing. They confiscated gambling paraphernalia: one copper [unclear character], forty-eight chips, thirty-two yuan in cash, three jiao in corner tickets, four thousand copper coins, and twenty-four jiao in small change. The witnesses were taken to the bureau. After Director Zhang interrogated each person, they all claimed not to know the name of the gambling boss. An examination of the household registration records revealed that the householder was Zhu Zhaokui from Shaoxing, who had fled upon hearing the news. The witnesses were ordered to be sent to the headquarters for interrogation, and a search warrant was issued for the arrest of the gambling boss.

Epidemic Spreads in This City; Last Week's Mortality Rate Was Three Hundred and Ninety-Two Cases with Eighty-Three Deaths

As autumn deepens and the weather suddenly turns cold, various epidemics are spreading rapidly. According to the reports on infectious disease mortality released last week by the Seaport Quarantine Office, the Public Concession Public Works Department's Health Department, and the French Concession Municipal Council Health Department, the following were reported:

Fifty-seven cases of typhoid and paratyphoid fever, with thirty-two deaths. One hundred and seventy-three cases of dysentery, with twenty-one deaths. Twenty cases of diphtheria, with four deaths. Twenty-six cases of pulmonary tuberculosis, with twenty-three deaths. Four cases of beriberi, with three deaths. The remaining cases include nine cases of scarlet fever and five cases of influenza. Eighty-two cases of malaria, but no deaths. In total, there were three hundred and ninety-two cases and eighty-three deaths.

Grand Opening of the Huxi Domestic Goods Department Store Yesterday; Liang Sisters Cut the Ribbon; Citizens Enthusiastically Visit

The Huxi Domestic Currency Department Store held its grand opening ceremony yesterday afternoon. Liang Saizhen cut the ribbon, and Liang Saishan unveiled the plaque.

Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the department store held its opening ceremony on Carter Road. Attendees included actresses Liang Saizhen and Liang Saishan, Cao Zhigong of the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession, Zhang Yichen of the National Physical Education Association, Liu Zhongying of the Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association, Chen Jiufeng of the Leather Goods Industry Association, Hu Fengxiang of the First Special District Citizens Federation, Ge Futian of the Nantong Fellow-Villagers Association, and approximately two hundred others, chaired by Xie Baosheng.

Ribbon Cutting and Unveiling

After the ceremonial rites, the chairman accompanied the Liang sisters as they cut the red and green ribbons at the entrance to the strains of music. Then, Liang Saishan pulled back the curtain covering the main entrance, unveiling the plaque. The crowd entered in droves amidst thunderous applause, and participating manufacturers began their business at that moment.

Chairman's Report

The opening ceremony was then held in the auditorium. Chairman Xie Baosheng reported, "Distinguished guests, comrades, we are extremely honored to have you attend the opening of this department store today. We are particularly fortunate to have the presence of Misses Liang Saizhen and Liang Saishan, who are presiding over the ribbon-cutting and unveiling ceremonies. In recent years, our country has suffered from the economic invasion of foreign powers, leading to the decline of our domestic industries. Although the industrial and commercial sectors have strived to improve, the lack of discerning ability among the populace has resulted in a failure to reduce the annual surplus of foreign goods. The purpose of this department store exhibition is to provide an opportunity for producers and consumers to jointly promote industry and revive our economy. It is hoped that from now on, the industrial sector will strive to improve manufacturing, and consumers will increase their support of domestic goods."

Declaration

The department store issued a declaration stating, "Our country's material progress lags behind its craftsmanship. As foreign goods are sold alongside domestic products in the market, buyers lack the ability to distinguish between them, or they shift their gaze and happily use foreign goods. Only by centrally promoting domestic goods can we arouse the interest of customers. The area of Huxi is densely populated and vast, and it is urgent to expand as much as possible to meet the needs of all sectors of Huxi, allowing them to purchase nearby. We have specifically created this department store to collect the best domestic products. Please do not underestimate the insignificance of individual purchases. It should be known that 'many hands make light work,' and 'many a little makes a mickle.' If everyone has the same heart and fulfills their patriotic duties, it is not impossible to stem the tide of foreign goods."

Divisional Display

The interior of the department store is divided into more than thirty sections, including silk fabrics, cloth head, camel [unclear character], fashionable coats, boots and shoes, wool textiles, socks, clothing, [unclear character] shirts, water bottles, cosmetics, felt hats, wool yarn, glass products, leather goods, domestic umbrellas, enamelware, ginseng and swallow's nest, lottery tickets, handkerchiefs, native produce, silver shields, miscellaneous goods, stationery, toys, copper and iron beds, snacks, fresh fruits, sweets, wild game, etc. The exhibition will last for six months, and it is planned to set up an entertainment section to enhance the interest of visitors.

News from Trade Associations

Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association, due to the rampant offering of excessively low bids by fellow businesses, which has disrupted industry regulations, issued a notice to all members yesterday. The original text of the notice is recorded below:

"Notice: It has been reported that recently, fellow businesses have been soliciting dyeing orders from various silk shops and silk and satin foreign goods shops, using a voting-style method to set dyeing prices at excessively low rates. In addition, there are unscrupulous street runners who deliberately offer prices far below cost, in order to undermine business and sow doubt among silk manufacturers, intending to cause disruption. All of these are detrimental to the entire industry's overall dyeing prices and overall business. The impact will only lead to the further decline of our industry to the point of no return. It is necessary to warn against cunning and deceit."

"The association discussed this matter at the 18th Executive Supervisory Committee meeting on the 4th of this month. The consensus was that 'This kind of unfair competition not only destroys business, but also harms oneself and the industry. The malicious intent is extremely regrettable. From now on, if any fellow business solicits orders from the silk industry with excessively low bids through a bidding-style method, causing damage to the standard dyeing prices set by the entire industry, upon investigation and confirmation, the member will be held fully liable for all damages incurred, in accordance with the oath made in their voluntary statement, and will be prosecuted according to law without leniency. As for the silk shops' requests for dyeing price lists, all fellow businesses must first create and submit the lists to the association. After the association reviews them, they may be sent out; otherwise, price discrepancies will cause suspicion and harm the business. Violations of the industry regulations should also be thoroughly investigated."

"The above resolution has been passed. This important notice is hereby recorded, and all members must strictly comply."

The Shanghai Northern District Engraving Industry Association held its 25th Executive Committee meeting at 4 PM on the 4th. Executive Committee members Fan Zhiheng, Meng Jiale, Yang Zhitian, Song Zhengyuan, Han Zumin, Xu Guanfu, and Qiu Shengshou were present. B. Issue a fixed-term appeal for fellow businesses to join the association. (Resolved) Set the period from October 10th to October 31st as the period for appealing to join the association. Those who do not comply after the deadline will be dealt with according to the central government's sanctions.

C. [Omitted]

D. Appoint additional investigators to intensify investigative affairs. (Resolved) Approved.

E. Penalize executive committee members for not attending meetings. (Resolved) Approved. The meeting adjourned.

Sash Factory Industry

The Shanghai Sash Factory Industry Association held an Executive Committee meeting at the China National Products Maintenance Association on the afternoon of the 3rd. More than ten people, including Weng Jingfu and Wu Fengyi, were present. Wu Fengyi chaired the meeting. The following results were achieved:

(1) Solicit those fellow businesses who have not yet joined to join.

(2) The association's office will be temporarily located at the China National Products Maintenance Association, pending further negotiations.

(3) The association's expenses will be one yuan and five jiao per month for member factories and one yuan per month for member factories. Yao Yunsheng was appointed to be responsible for receipts and disbursements.

(4) The Executive Committee will hold a meeting on the 2nd and 16th of each month.

(5) All committee members must join the Kuomintang. The meeting adjourned.

Since ending the epidemic prevention injections on the 15th of last month, the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau began the vaccination campaign the following day. Since the Municipal Health Bureau began the vaccination campaign on the 16th of last month, it has been sending two doctors and two nurses to various schools in the city every day for vaccinations. Elementary School Principal Punished for Fraudulent Fundraising: Donating in the Name of the Shicai Association; Fined One Hundred Yuan

The Shanghai Chengji Shicai Charity Association previously raised funds from all walks of life for the purpose of providing coffins. Its address was located at No. 1163, Tonghe Lane, Wuding Road. However, the charity association closed down the year before last, and all documents, seals, origins, etc., were kept by Peng Kangnian, a member of the association from Suzhou. Peng opened the Huimeng Elementary School at No. 49, Lane 781, Xinzha Road, and served as its principal. However, starting in April of this year, Peng suddenly had malicious intentions and continued to use the name of the Chengji Shicai Charity Association, assigning Jiang Jinqing, a former member of the association from Changzhou, to solicit donations from businesses with a donation book. The proceeds were split between them. At around 10 AM the day before yesterday, Jiang went to the home of Wang Shiqing at No. 26, Taili Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, to solicit donations. Wang agreed to donate one yuan, but he needed to check with the association to verify its authenticity. Unexpectedly, Jiang fled, and Wang reported this to Chinese Constable No. 1735, who took Jiang, along with the donation book, receipt, origin, newspaper, etc., to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. Under investigation by Chinese Detective Wang Wenbin, Peng Kangnian was subsequently arrested at the Huimeng Elementary School on Xinzha Road, and seven seals were confiscated and taken back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu prosecuted them for fraud under Article 339 of the Criminal Code and presented the above circumstances. Jiang Jinqing admitted to soliciting donations on Peng's orders and that he had collected more than thirty yuan from April to the present, of which he gave Peng more than ten yuan. Peng Kangnian denied conspiring with Jiang, making evasive statements, and retained a lawyer to defend him. After verifying the statements, Judge Pan Zhenyang sentenced Jiang Jinqing and Peng Kangnian to joint continuous fraud, with a fine of one hundred yuan each. If they were to serve labor service, it would be calculated at two yuan per day. The receipts and seals were confiscated.

Performing Artist Accused of Abusing Female Apprentice

Beiping - Wu Gong performing artist Zhang Debing, stage name Gaitianhong, age 22, recently came to Shanghai from Jiangxi after his troupe disbanded, residing at 40 Baokang Lane, Avenue Joffre, French Concession. Zhang married Wu, a Shaoxing woman (18 years old this year), two years ago. In October of last year, through introductions from his wife's family, he took in Wang Huahua, a 12-year-old girl from Lanxi, as his apprentice, teaching her Wu Gong opera arts. During training, beatings with sticks and hands were unavoidable. Zhang's wife, Wu, young and quick-tempered, also frequently beat the girl, causing discontent among the neighbors. The French police received a report letter the day before, alleging Zhang's abuse of his female apprentice. Detective Zhou Ruiyuan was dispatched to investigate and found bruises on both sides of the girl Wang Huahua's cheeks and soreness in her right arm, confirming the assault. Zhang was arrested and, along with the girl, taken back to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Special District, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the hearing. Gu Shouxi, a lawyer representing the police department, presented the case and requested an extension for further investigation before proceeding with the trial. Subsequently, the girl Wang Huahua testified that her master usually treated her well, and only lightly disciplined her when she didn't perform well in training. However, she stated that her mistress was very fierce and often beat her. She said she did not want to report on her master but wanted her mistress to be investigated. Questioned, the defendant Zhang Debing denied the abuse and beatings. Zhang's wife, Wu, was listening outside the court and was summoned for questioning. She admitted to occasionally scolding and hitting the girl for breaking bowls and dishes. The court reviewed the testimonies and adjourned the hearing to the 12th for further investigation, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

Xu Bokang Arrested for Concealing Opium

Xu Bokang, a grain merchant from Wuxi, residing at 22 Zhujiaqiao, French Concession, was found at 4:30 PM the day before, concealing seven packages of opium, totaling six and a half taels. He was riding the No. 18 trolleybus when, near the intersection of Dongyouheng Road and Zhaofeng Road, he was stopped by Chinese detectives Lin Aizhong and Xu Bingnan of the Huishan Police Department, along with Chinese constable No. 2051, who found his behavior suspicious and arrested him. Xu claimed that the opium belonged to Yuan Shisheng, residing at 42 Kaifeng Road, who had asked him to deliver it to 30, Lane 783, Zhoujiajui Road. The detectives rushed to Kaifeng Road but couldn't find Yuan. They then went to 30 Anle Lane, Zhoujiajui Road, and apprehended two Ningbo men, Lin Yunzhang, and Anhui man, Zhu Huazai, who were consuming opium, along with their opium paraphernalia. All were taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Fifth Criminal Court of the First Special District. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian presented the case and requested an investigation. Detective Sun then reported the details of the arrest and presented the evidence. Questioned, Xu Bokang confessed that a friend, Lin Genbao, had asked him to deliver the opium in a "triangular" trade, offering vague explanations and begging for leniency. The two defendants, Lin and Zhu, denied knowing Xu and claimed to have quit opium a long time ago. Judge Zhan ordered them to be remanded in custody, pending sentencing.

Caojiadu Police Station Arrests Gambling Syndicate Members

Wang Zhenxin, 36 years old from Nanxiang, residing at 41 Xin Gongyi Lane, Rue de Zikawei, Shanghai West, specialized in running "flower society" betting dens in the Shanghai West area, enticing people to gamble. Recently, due to carelessness, his activities were discovered by Inspector Liu Pei of the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau. Inspector Liu, along with Inspector Li, led police officers to the location quietly. They arrested Wang on the spot and confiscated numerous "flower society" ledgers, betting slips, and gambling funds. Wang confessed without hesitation, while Li and the others denied any knowledge. The bureau deemed Wang and his accomplices to be extremely unlawful in establishing "flower society" betting dens to swindle money. They prepared a document to be sent to the main bureau for further investigation.

Partner Flees After Failure, Court Orders Arrest of Ji Yi

Ji Yi, a lawyer from Anhui who had withdrawn from the bar association, was recently sued in the Second Special District Court by Wang Zhenhua, a former county magistrate, who hired a lawyer to claim that Ji Yi had defrauded him of 1,500 yuan last winter under the guise of a joint speculative venture. Based on the complaint, the court, presided over by Judge Sun Pengxian, summoned Ji Yi and ordered him to provide a guarantor who would ensure his appearance. Ji Yi's younger brother, Ji Qizong, persuaded Gao Yaozhang, a Suzhou native residing at 9 Liuxian Village, Avenue du Maréchal Joffre, to entrust Chen Yifei, the owner of Tianle Tailor Shop at 2 Yushun Lane, Dongxin Bridge Street, to vouch for Ji Yi for 15 days, falsely claiming that Ji Yi was involved in a fight. Chen, being illiterate, rashly agreed and provided a written guarantee. However, after Ji Yi was released on bail, he claimed illness and disappeared without a trace. Chen Yifei learned that Ji Yi was charged with fraud and requested the withdrawal of his guarantee. The Second Special District Court transferred the case to the prosecutor's office and detained Gao and Chen for questioning, ordering them to provide Ji Yi. This matter has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Sun again presided over the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. Wang Zhenhua accused Ji Yi of fraud, but the defendant was absent. The court ordered the arrest of Ji Yi for further investigation.

Rickshaw Driver's Bestial Act

Du Jinxiang, a police officer at post No. 33, Xinkou, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, was approached at around 10 AM yesterday by Shen Shaofu, a resident of the area, who accused Liu Baohua of raping his ten-year-old daughter, causing injuries and bleeding. Shen also presented several bloodstained pairs of pants. Police Officer Du arrested the accused and, along with the victim, took them to the Zhongxing Road Police Station. Inspector Xie Zhong conducted the investigation. Shen Shaofu, 33 years old from Chongming, residing at the rear building of 12 Tongxing Lane, Qiujiang Road, and working as a rickshaw puller, stated that his twelve-year-old daughter, Mao Nv, was currently studying at a nearby primary school. On the morning of the first of this month, at around 7 AM, Shen had left to pull his rickshaw, and Mao Nv was still asleep in the room. Liu Baohua, a friend living in the front building, snuck into the room and raped Mao Nv, causing injuries and incessant bleeding. Initially, Shen suspected it was her menstruation but, realizing the situation was wrong, he forced his daughter to reveal the truth and arrested the accused, presenting the bloodstained pants as evidence, requesting severe punishment, adding that Liu Baohua was also a friend. Shen Mao Nv testified that she was thirteen years old and currently attending school. Liu Baohua covered her mouth to prevent her from making noise and removed her lower clothing. She was unable to resist and was violated. Her lower body was swollen and bleeding incessantly. She was still asleep at the time, and no one was upstairs. The door was also tightly closed by Liu, so she was helpless and had to endure the act. Liu Baohua, 33 years old from Haimen, admitted to being a friend of Shen Shaofu and also working in the same trade, pulling a rickshaw at Zifeng Money Exchange, 240 Ningbo Road, but was evasive about the rest. After reviewing the testimonies, the interrogating officer immediately reported the case to the Xinzha Sub-bureau. The bureau, deeming the case to involve the rape of a minor, ordered it to be transferred to the Public Security Bureau. It was learned that the Public Security Bureau had taken custody of the suspect at around 5 PM yesterday for further investigation.

Fire at Tiediqiao, Pudong

Two rooms rented by a Zhang from Chongming, without a street number, at Tiediqiao, Pudong, caught fire yesterday morning around 11 AM when Zhang was cooking. The fire quickly spread, and the family escaped in haste. Another three tenants were living in the house, Fan Wu (55 years old) from Tiantai, making a living by farming. He had returned from the field in the morning, had breakfast, and was fast asleep. He woke up screaming when the flames touched him. At that moment, the Pudong Fire Brigade was returning from putting out a fire in a thatched hut in Yangjia, north of Tiediqiao, which fortunately did not cause significant damage. Seeing the fire at Tiediqiao, they rushed to the scene. Firefighters braved the flames and rescued Fan Wu, who was severely burned, with skin peeling off, hair charred, and face lacerated, unconscious. He was rushed to Pudong Hospital, where his condition was critical. The two thatched huts were reduced to ashes in an instant. The Zhang family, fearing punishment, fled without a trace.

Child Argues Over Picture Card, Father Slashes Head - Boxing Master's Violent Assault

Luo Chunfa, a resident of 1 Dexin Road, Zhabei, originally from Huzhou, had a son, Changgen, eight years old, who was arguing with Yang Xiaogou over picking up cigarette cards yesterday afternoon around 5 PM. They started fighting, and Yang's left middle finger was bitten by Luo's son, causing him extreme pain and crying loudly. His father, Yang Jintao, a boxing master known for his violent temper, heard about his son's bitten finger and flew into a rage. He grabbed a steel saber used for practice and rushed to Luo's house. Without asking any questions, he slashed Luo twice, once on the left shoulder and once on the forehead, cutting away about two inches of flesh, causing profuse bleeding. The police investigated and arrested both men. The injured man was taken to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Steamed Bun and Pancake Factory Planned - Survey of Over Two Hundred Shops - Fundraising in Progress

According to Guomin She, most working-class people in this city have limited income, and their main food consists of steamed buns and pancakes. There are no fewer than three hundred shops in the city selling these foods, but the production and operation are highly unreasonable. The sales scope has been decreasing, lacking a balanced adjustment mechanism. Furthermore, due to inefficient methods, they cannot handle large-scale business, and after being exploited, they can hardly survive. To rescue the situation and improve this business, a centralized steamed bun and pancake factory is planned for the entire city. The plan aims to rationalize production and operation, improve the quality of products, help most shops reduce losses, and expand the sales of these foods. A survey has been conducted among over two hundred existing shops in the city, soliciting their opinions, and they all support the idea. Fundraising is now actively underway, and the factory is expected to be established in the shortest possible time. Anyone wishing to know more about this detailed plan or to discuss it should contact Mr. Hai Bibo directly at 232 Po Sai Road.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: Shandong and the Yellow River basin will be clear and cool, with southwest to northwest winds. The middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River will be cloudy with rain and light, unstable winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River will be mostly clear, gradually becoming cloudy, with light southwest to southeast winds. The East China Sea and Taiwan will have rain with gentle north to east winds. Also, the maximum temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 81.0 degrees, and the minimum temperature was 62.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the maximum temperature was 79.9 degrees, and the minimum temperature was 65.8 degrees.

Business News

Finance - Bullion Speculators Switch from Buying to Selling

The gold market was very calm yesterday, with both pure gold and foreign exchange. Prices rose initially, but unexpectedly, speculators sold high, causing the exchange rate to ease and gradually decline. In the morning, the overseas silver market saw the British pound rise and the U.S. dollar unchanged. The Montreal forward silver price remained unchanged or rose by one cent. The foreign exchange rate was slightly reduced. The London spot gold price remained unchanged. The Central Bank's official rate remained unchanged for both British and U.S. currencies. The customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard bullion price was still listed at 1146.6 yuan. In pre-market trading, the price opened slightly lower at 55 yuan. Qiafeng Yongtai, Decheng, Chunyuan, and Yongfen all rose to around 57 yuan. The market opened high, and both long and short positions chased gains, causing prices to continue to rise. Hengyu took advantage of the high prices to aggressively sell, and speculators switched from buying to selling, gradually pushing prices lower. There was still much consolidation in the middle. The HSBC exchange rate remained unchanged for both British and U.S. currencies, and the silver equalization tax rose by 0.75, but these had no impact. Supply exceeded demand in the market, and the trend turned weak, gradually declining. However, there was still much support at the lower prices. Although spot dealers were selling, the overall trend was still stable. However, Chinese merchants were psychologically weak and sold foreign exchange, causing the exchange rate to continue to ease. The market lacked support. Indian silver first report rose by 1.2.2 anna, but there was much consolidation despite the rise. The Indian silver second report remained unchanged, and finally turned stable after weakening. The market situation for the day is recorded below.

The morning opened at 1156.7 yuan, up 2 yuan from last Saturday. Dadecheng, Fuxing, Yonghengchang, and Yongfen bought, rising to 8.5 yuan. Hengyu, Yuxinxiang, Chunyuan, and Yong sold, falling to 6.4 yuan. Hengyu, Fuxing, and Yong bought at the lower prices, rising to 7.7 yuan. After that, the HSBC exchange rate remained unchanged for both British and U.S. currencies, and the silver equalization tax was announced to be up 0.75, but these had no impact. Chunyuan, Yonghengyu, Tianfa, Zhengchang, and Dadecheng Yuanmao Yong jointly sold, gradually falling to 4.5 yuan. Fuda, Fuxing, and Yong came in to buy, rising to 5.4 yuan. Yuanmao Yong, Dafeng Heng, and retail investors continued to supply, causing the price to drop to 4.3 yuan. Yuanmao Yong and Tongtaichang maintained support at the lower prices. The noon close was at 1154.9 yuan.

The afternoon opened at 1154.8 yuan. Dingkang, Hengyu, and Dadecheng added, rising to 5.7 yuan. Jin, Yong, Fuxing, Yong, Yuanmao Yong, and Qiafeng Yong sold, falling to 4.5 yuan. Demao Yong bought at the lower prices, rising to 5.1 yuan. Yuanmao Yong sold to 4.4 yuan. Dadecheng bought again, rising to 4.9 yuan. Tianfa, Yuanmao Yong, Dachangxiang, and Hengyu sold, falling to 2.5 yuan. Yuanmao Yong and Chunyuan Yong added, rising to 3.3 yuan. The domestic market was still strong, and Dachangxiang and Hengyu Yuanmao Yong sold, falling to 3 yuan. Qiafeng Yong, Yuanmao Yong, and Chunyuan Yong bought again at the lower prices, rising again to 3.2 yuan. After consolidation, the closing price was 1153.1 yuan. The market was stable after the close.

The settlement price was still listed at the Central Bank's standard bullion price of 1146.6 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it was about 17 yuan lower. The account for this month was 1150 yuan, and for November it was 1155 yuan. The spot market was stable. Tianjin goods were priced at an additional 13.5 yuan, and red-hot goods were bid at 12 yuan, but no transactions were made. Sheng Yuanyong sold over 200 taels of red-hot goods to silversmiths at an additional 17.5 yuan. Sheng Yuanyong sold seven spot bullion bars to outsiders at a discount of 2 yuan, totaling 1156 yuan. The spot price for November delivery was discounted by Sheng Yuanyong to Chengda at 2 yuan for 70 bars, and by Dachangxiang to Qiafengyong at 2.5 yuan for 28 bars. In the after-market, Dafengheng discounted to Chengda at 2 yuan for 56 bars.

There were uncertain transactions in the market. In summary, Dingkang, Qiafeng Yong, Fuxing Yong, Chunyuan Yong, Tongtaichang, Shenda Yonghengchang, Yongjiu Dafu, and Dayuanmao Yong were buyers. Hengyu, Dachangxiang, Shengyuan Yongtong, Fenghheng Dafengheng, Qingfa Yongcheng, Da Yuxinxiang, and Feng were sellers. Dadecheng Fu Yu advanced first and then came out, and Shunmao Yuanmao Yong came out first and then went in.

Looking at the market situation for the day, it went from stable to weak. The morning opened at 1156.7 yuan, and the after-hours closed at 1153.1 yuan. The highest price was 1158.5 yuan, and the lowest price was 1152 yuan, a difference of 6.5 yuan. As a result, the price fell by 1.6 yuan compared to the previous close. There were still 490 bars left for this month, with a total of seven long positions and six short positions. There were 8,722 November futures contracts, with a total of 36 long positions and 32 short positions. The transaction volume was 4,781 bars in the first half of the day and 2,492 bars in the afternoon.

Chinese Merchants Sell U.S. Dollars

The exchange market was characterized yesterday by Chinese merchants selling more than 800,000 U.S. dollars, with forward rates rising. In the morning, overseas reports indicated that London large strips rose by 1.25 for both near and distant months. The New York silver market was closed, and the Montreal forward silver price was unchanged or up by one cent. London spot gold was unchanged, the British pound to U.S. dollar rate was unchanged, the British pound to French franc rate fell by 28 points, the U.S. dollar to British pound rate fell by 1.25, and the British pound to U.S. dollar rate rose by 8.75. The Central Bank's official rates remained unchanged for both British and U.S. currencies, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The exchange market opened with near-term selling prices of one shilling, two pence, and 3125 for British exchange and 29.4375 yuan for U.S. exchange. Compared to the previous close, British exchange was slightly easier, while U.S. exchange was 0.0625 weaker. After opening, the Oriental and Great Britain banks took the lead, and other banks followed suit. The HSBC exchange rate remained unchanged for both British and U.S. currencies. There was much consolidation in the process. The silver equalization tax was announced to be up 0.75. Afterwards, Chinese commercial banks made sales, and the situation gradually eased. But even though the banks took the lead, forward rates remained firm at noon. In the after-market, Chinese merchants continued to sell, and the market remained easy. However, banks maintained support at the lower prices, resulting in a struggle. Indian silver first report rose by 1.2.2 anna, the second report was unchanged, and finally it was mediocre. At the close, near-term selling prices were one shilling, two pence, 34375 and 375 for British exchange, and 29.5 yuan for U.S. exchange. Compared to last Saturday, British exchange was slightly easier and U.S. exchange was unchanged. In terms of forward rates, British exchange was 1.25 easier and U.S. exchange was 15625 stronger. The day's transactions are recorded below.

British exchange opened in the morning at one shilling, two pence, and 3125. China-Belgian sold 21875 to Oriental for December, and Shanghai-Belgian sold to Great Britain at the same price for the same month. China-Belgian went long for January at 21875, and Oriental sold spot at 375 to Citibank. In the after-market, HSBC went long for December at 28125, and Youli also went long for the same month at the same price. Mitsui Youli sold to HSBC for October at 34375. The closing selling prices were one shilling, two pence, 375 and 34375 for spot, 3125 and 375 for October, 3125 for November, 25 and 3125 for December, and 25 for January. The buying price was adjusted upwards.

U.S. exchange opened with a near-term selling price of 29.4375 yuan. HSBC Continental sold to Jincheng for January at 0625, and Maccallum Sayer sold 1875 for December and 125 for January, going long for March at 29 yuan. Citibank took 375 for November and 25 for December. Shanghai-Sayer spot was half, and Maccallum Citibank went long for December at 3125. Shanghai went long for January at 25. The near-term selling price at noon was 29.5 yuan. In the after-market, Maccallum went long for December at 3125, Zhengjin added for January at 25, Youli went long for December at 3125, and Mitsui China-Belgian also went long at the same price for the same month. The closing price was 29.5 yuan for spot, 4375 for October, 375 for November, 25 and 3125 for December, and 1875 and 25 for January. The buying price was adjusted upwards by 0625.

Securities Forward Government Bonds Experience a Stronger Downturn

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange market was extremely volatile, and people were also very uneasy. Mr. Sangshima's arrival in China has already led to a hurried transfer from Shanghai to Beijing. The negotiations with Japan seem to be reaching the final stage. Opinions differ, and it is difficult to grasp whether the news is positive or negative. Although the market appears tight, it cannot withstand the impact of rumors. Although the situation feels tense, it is all demonstrative action. The future of the market is likely to see a larger range of fluctuation. Yesterday, the market opened in the morning with prices still tight. Category D rose sharply by about ten cents, while the rest were up by a small five cents to three cents. Sellers were mostly offering November and 16 bonds, while buyers were most eager for number 4. When the market opened in the afternoon, numbers 5 and 51 were also being sold. Except for categories 1 and 2, which remained slightly firm by five cents, most others continued to decline by a small five cents to a dime or two and a half cents. At closing, there were some unfounded rumors, and retail investors sold heavily, causing a further decline of five cents to a dime or three cents. Since the currency reform, the foundation of government bonds has become more solid than before. Therefore, although the number of chips has increased significantly, market price fluctuations have been less severe than before because government bonds are equivalent to legal tender. Yesterday's market price results showed that Categories E, D, and C rose slightly, from five cents to three and a half cents, while the long-term Category C fell slightly by two cents, and Category A plummeted by as much as fifty-five cents. The total trading volume was 12,490,000 yuan. The results of the price increases and decreases are compared in the table on the left (unit: yuan, trading unit: 100 yuan).

Cotton Yarn Sales to Sichuan are Strong

The yarn market has turned firmer, and the situation is rising again. The situation has eased and short positions have been covered. At the same time, the spot yarn supply is still tight and sales to Sichuan have improved. As a result, people's confidence has recovered and the market has turned from decline to briskness. However, it has been found that various parties have handled 40,000 to 50,000 bales, of which November futures yarn accounts for 20,000 bales. The future situation is difficult to predict.

Long Positions in Futures Yarn Increase Their Bets

At the opening of the futures yarn market, all months rose in unison. Due to the easing of the situation and the stabilization of people's sentiment, there was a lack of sellers in the market, and the momentum became tighter. The second round was slightly weaker. By the third round, large players were covering short positions and gold firms were increasing their long positions. At the same time, sales to Sichuan Province were active, and the market atmosphere suddenly became tense. Market prices then moved forward. It was found that Yu Da, De Da, Ming De, Shen Ji, Tai Chang, and Run Kang were selling, while Geng Feng, Xing Chang, Da Chang Cheng, and Tong He were buying heavily. As a result, all months rose by 1.50 to 2 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. At the opening in the afternoon, it was heard that yarn sales to Sichuan Province were strong, people's sentiment was high, and the market rose sharply. As a result, near-month prices rose 25 cents compared to the morning closing price, while far-month prices fell 10 cents. It was found that Yu Da sold 5,900 bales, De Da 1,510 bales, Ju Xing 1,400 bales, Shen Ji 1,150 bales, Tai Chang 2,450 bales, Run Kang 1,100 bales, and Xie Cheng 1,300 bales. On the buying side, Zhen Da bought 1,500 bales, Geng Feng 5,650 bales, Xing Chang 4,000 bales, Da Chang Cheng 4,250 bales, Chang Feng 1,650 bales, Tong He 2,150 bales, Tong Ji 1,300 bales, and Heng Yi 1,300 bales. Futures Cotton Sees Significant Short Covering

Cotton cloth prices rebounded due to the good yarn market and significant short covering, which dried up the market. Market prices gradually rose. However, the overseas cotton market is trending softer.

Cotton Prices Rise Gradually

At the opening of the futures cotton market, because U.S. cotton continued to fall by 6 to 8 points and Indian cotton was also sluggish, with Osaka Three-Product cotton falling by 2.3 yuan, the market was mediocre, with each month rising slightly by 5 to 10 cents. Unexpectedly, in the second round, due to the rise in the yarn market, Feng Jin Chang suddenly came in to purchase in bulk, and supply was temporarily unable to meet demand. Market prices suddenly jumped up by 35 cents. The situation remained good until the third closing, with prices continuing to rise by 5 to 10 cents. Sellers Yi Kang, Yu Da, Chang Feng, Run Kang, Feng Tai, Yi Chang, Chang He, and Da Fu all sold in small quantities. Only Feng Jin bought more than 21,000 dan, and Jin Chang also purchased more than 11,000 dan. Da Chang Cheng, Jin Chang, Xing Chang, and Da also covered short positions significantly. As a result, prices for all months rose by 30 to 45 cents compared to the previous day's closing price. At the opening in the afternoon, the near-month prices were flat, but the far-month prices were still good. There was not much change in the second and third rounds, but the momentum was very tight due to large players covering short positions. The closing was particularly firm. As a result, prices for all months rose again by 10 to 20 cents compared to the morning closing price, with the near month falling by 5 cents. It was found that Chang Feng sold 12,200 dan, Yi Chang 5,400 dan, Run Kang 3,000 dan, Xin Cheng 4,200 dan, Feng Tai 2,500 dan, Da Kang 2,300 dan, Yuan Da 3,900 dan, Yu Da 6,300 dan, Ju 3,100 dan, Chang He 12,600 dan, Yi Kang 2,400 dan, and Hua Mao 2,000 dan. Jin Chang bought 13,100 dan, Feng 34,700 dan, Jin Chang 5,800 dan, Tong He 2,600 dan, Yuan Xing Chang 3,200 dan, Tai Xing 4,100 dan, Da Chang Cheng 2,400 dan, and Zhen Da 2,700 dan. The daily high and low market prices are listed below.
